Qingdao Implements Recovery of Fishing Rights 103

Fishing Company Officially Opens

Japanese Residents United in Attempting Resistance

Qingdao Correspondence: Due to the long-term monopoly of the fishing industry in Jiaozhou Bay by the Japanese, the Qingdao Chamber of Commerce, in order to recover lost rights, has united with various sectors to establish a fishing joint-stock company. The original capital was set at 500,000 yuan, divided into 10,000 shares, each worth 50 yuan. In addition to the 5,000 shares held by the company's promoters, the remaining shares have been gradually subscribed by various sectors. The Chamber of Commerce has also recommended fifteen people, including Chairman Song Yuting, to be preparatory committee members. They have submitted a request to the Municipal Government to allocate two plots of official land on Heze Road and Xiaogang Road as the foundation for the establishment of a fish market and cold storage facility. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce has also telegraphed the Central Executive Yuan and various ministries, requesting that they order the Jiaohai Customs to faithfully implement central orders and strictly control foreign fishing vessels within the specified limits to protect the fishing industry and regain sovereignty. It is reported that the company, eager to start operations, has temporarily leased a private house on Xiaogang Road and officially held its opening ceremony on May 1st. Over a thousand people attended, including representatives from Party and government agencies, various organizations, and fish merchants. After the meeting began, Chairman Song Yuting first reported on the company's preparatory progress. Then, representatives Wang Chaofan, Zhou Jiayan, Yang Jinsheng, and Yu Jinhe successively delivered speeches, praising the company and encouraging them to work hard to recover fishing rights and wash away the previous humiliation. After the meeting, fish merchants began trading. However, it is reported that the Japanese side has been paying close attention. Most of the Japanese residents in Qingdao are engaged in fishing. If our plan is implemented, they will all be unemployed. They have secretly organized a fishing navigation maintenance association, hoping to resist. They have also sent seven representatives to the Japanese consulate to request assistance. Japanese Deputy Consul Mochizuki promised to accept their request. Indeed, the Japanese are unwilling to give up their right to invade territorial waters and fish illegally. (May 2nd)

Jiaoji Railway Implements Fare and Freight Increase 104

Drafting Fourteen Provisional Measures

Qingdao Correspondence: The Jiaoji Railway, following the resolution of the Ministry of Railways, will increase passenger and freight transportation rates by 20% uniformly starting from May 1st. Fourteen provisional measures for the price increase have been drafted and notified by the Transportation Department to all sections and stations for implementation. They are transcribed as follows: (1) The fare increase should be 20% on the original price of ordinary passenger tickets. For discounted tickets, the increase should be 20% on the actual amount paid. A stamp of "Price Increase 20%" should be added to the ticket. Luggage, parcels, vehicles, livestock, express trains, sleeper berths, platform tickets, postal delivery and storage fees, vehicle rental fees, and miscellaneous income will not be increased. (2) The 20% fare increase should be calculated to the nearest cent. If the fraction is less than one cent, it should be rounded up to one cent. However, for supplementary tickets, the minimum is five cents, so if it is less than five cents, five cents should be charged, and if it is less than one dime, one dime should be charged. (3) For season tickets and return tickets, the price increase should be collected in one payment at the time of sale and stamped. (4) For round-trip tickets, the price increase for both journeys should be collected by the departure station in one payment. (5) For those traveling without a ticket or exceeding the class or station, a 20% increase should be added to the supplementary ticket price. The penalty should be calculated together with the price increase and clearly stated on the ticket. (6) For through tickets, only the fare due to this railway should be increased by 20% and stamped. If the other railway has not collected the 20% increase, it should be collected by the connecting station. If there is an omission, the ticket inspector on the train should collect it, issuing a supplementary ticket for proof. (7) The Department will print an express train price increase table and distribute it to all stations. When selling first and second-class express train tickets, the ordinary fare should be increased by 20%, and then the express train fare should be added. The ticket should be stamped with both "Passenger Ticket Price Increase 20%" and "Express Train Fee Not Increased." (8) For ordinary freight, the rate should be calculated first, and then 20% should be added to the freight amount due. For special freight, the freight discount should be calculated first, then the freight amount due should be calculated by the ton, and then 20% should be added. The freight bills must be filled out separately for verification and stamped with a 20% price increase. Livestock, boats, sedan chairs, gold ingots, silver ingots, bank notes, locomotives, empty vehicles, delayed storage, shunting fees, and special line maintenance fees will not be increased. (9) The 20% freight increase should be calculated in cents. If the fraction is less than one cent, it should be rounded up to one cent. (10) The 20% price increase for freight bills payable and freight bills on account should be calculated and filled out by the departure station for verification by the arrival station and the accounting office. (11) When the freight on the freight bill needs to be corrected according to regulations, the price increase should be corrected accordingly. If there is a penalty, it should be calculated together with the price increase and filled out separately in the correction letter for verification. (12) For the price increase of through freight, the railway of origin should collect the increased freight of 20%. Freight coming in from other railways, should have the arriving station collect the amount of 20%. All increases should be noted on the freight bill. (13) If there are any omissions in the collection of this price increase, whether on the train or at the station, they should be made up according to regulations. (14) These measures will be abolished when the new freight rate table, which increases the freight rate by 20%, is produced and new tickets are issued to all stations for implementation. (April 29th)

Hubei Troops Encircle He Long's Remnants 105

Fan's Division Clears Out the Remaining Bandits of Cheng Kechun

Ji's Division Has Recaptured the Bandit Stronghold of Qiliping

Hankou Correspondence: After He Long's remnant bandits fled from Ziyou Donggong City to Xiaojia Weir and Xuejiaping, the bandit stronghold of Donggong City was recovered by Guo Xun's forces. Guo Xun's forces then advanced from Donggong City towards Xiaojia Weir and Xuejiaping. The 48th Division of Xu Yuanquan's forces dispatched two regiments, led by Li and Fu, from Nanqiao and Xujiaji, while the 51st Division of Fan Shisheng's forces also dispatched three regiments, led by Cao, Wang, and Chen, from Liujiaji and Lijia Dang, to encircle and suppress the bandit area. He Long's bandits, having suffered repeated heavy blows, have no more than four or five thousand remnants, with only one or two thousand firearms. They are currently trapped there, with depleted food and no reinforcements. Their annihilation is not far off. For ease of command, the Wuhan Headquarters has ordered Guo Xun to be responsible for command and set a deadline for clearing out the remaining bandits. Furthermore, Guo's forces have recovered Donggong City with great merit, and Guo was specially commended by telegram on the 2nd, stating, "The officers and soldiers of your unit have worked hard and achieved repeated victories. I hope you will take advantage of the victory and pursue the enemy to achieve the effect of total annihilation. I also hope you will boost morale and capture He Long alive to eliminate this great evil." Previously, the forces of Cheng Kechun in northern Hubei were defeated by the 51st Division of Fan Shisheng's forces, and the bandit leader Cheng Kechun was killed. The bandits scattered. Recently, Fan's division has repeatedly uncovered Red bandit organizations in Zaoyang and Zhangjiawan, and the important criminals captured have been executed. Yesterday, on the 2nd, the chief of staff of the division, Ding Teng, telegraphed the Wuhan Headquarters to report, stating, "According to surrendered Red bandits Lu Shishun and Fu Liangnu, after the Red bandit leader Cheng Kechun of Zaoyang was reported to have died of serious injuries, the bandit forces greatly decreased. According to the bandit's recent plan, about two to three hundred firearms from Xiangfan will be led by Zhao Ying to concentrate at Zhushipu in Xiang County to respond to He Long. I have taken precautions in advance and repeatedly uncovered Red Party organizations in Zaocheng, Zhangjiawan, Dongjinwan, and Zhushipu, and captured more than ten important criminals, including Kang Ciqiao and Jiang Yingjie, all of whom have been executed. Xiang and Zao are now exceptionally stable. Please set your mind at ease." After receiving the telegram, the Wuhan Headquarters replied with an order to continue searching for and suppressing the remaining bandits in order to completely eradicate them.

The bandits in the Henan-Hubei border area were entrenched in Xinjie, Laoshanpo, Bopi River, Qiliping, etc. The Soviet government of the Henan-Anhui-Hubei Special Zone was located in Qiliping. Li Mingzhong, the pacification superintendent of the Henan-Anhui-Hubei border area, supervised and ordered the various units to encircle and suppress the bandits, and they have recovered Xinjie, Laoshanpo, and Bopi River. On the 30th of last month, Ji Hongchang's forces also recovered Qiliping. Ji telegraphed the Wuhan Headquarters yesterday, reporting the recovery of Qiliping, stating, "After my unit engaged the bandits in battle at Tuan Shu Gang, the bandits failed to carry out their plan and were severely attacked by us. The bandits all fled in the southwest direction. This morning, I reorganized my troops and followed up to suppress them. The advance troops reached the high mountains north of Wang Xijiu, and the bandits suddenly surrounded my 88th Brigade. A part of the bandits also attacked our army. In addition to the 88th Brigade fighting bravely, the 92nd Brigade rushed to the rescue, bypassing and occupying the northeastern mountains of Wang Xijiu, and counterattacked the bandits from the rear. The bandits were unable to resist and fought fiercely for three hours. By 1:00 PM, Wang Xijiu was completely occupied. At that time, my 92nd Brigade also arrived, and I ordered the 88th Brigade to continue to suppress the bandits, and the 89th and 91st Brigades to advance from the left and right, and the three brigades attacked Qiliping from all sides. The bandits resisted stubbornly, but Qiliping was completely occupied by my 88th Brigade at 3:00 PM. The remnants of the bandits fled south, and the mountains west of Qiliping were occupied by my 91st Brigade, and the Dongshan was occupied by the 92nd Brigade. Each pursued for more than ten miles. In this battle, more than 3,000 bandits were killed and more than 300 were captured, including many female Red bandits. The 91st Brigade seized four mortars and one mountain gun, and more than a hundred rounds of mortar and mountain gun shells. The 92nd, 88th, and 89th Brigades all obtained a large number of bandit weapons and military supplies. The bandits fled to Xuanhuadian. I am now leading my troops forward to pursue and suppress them. I respectfully submit this report." Furthermore, Li Mingzhong, the pacification superintendent of the Henan-Anhui-Hubei border area, believed that after the recovery of various places, post-war work should be handled urgently. Yesterday, he specially telegraphed the Wuhan Headquarters, requesting that personnel be dispatched quickly to handle it, so that the Party, government, and military could advance simultaneously to maintain security in other areas. (May 2nd)

Proposal to Abolish Nanchang City 106

Educational Circles Petition for Preservation

Mayor Gong Has Submitted His Resignation

Nanchang Correspondence: Jiangxi Province has been affected by bandit disasters, with no income. This year, the deficit in government expenses is estimated to be more than 8 million yuan. The Local Reorganization Committee, in order to economize on expenses, concentrate financial resources, and provide sufficient funds for bandit suppression and post-war reconstruction, has adopted a policy of austerity for administrative expenses. Many superfluous agencies have been abolished and merged, such as the Provincial Security Bureau being merged with the Garrison Headquarters, the Entomology Bureau being merged with the Agricultural Experiment Station, and the National Goods Exhibition Hall and the Provincial Autonomous Preparatory Office being abolished. Currently, for the sake of cost-saving, there is a proposal to abolish the Nanchang Municipal Government and have the four departments of Civil Affairs, Finance, Education, and Construction take over its responsibilities. After the municipal elementary schools learned of the Municipal Government's abolition plan, they held an emergency meeting on the 25th at the 24th Elementary School. More than a hundred people attended, including Ouyang Qin. Wang Anbo presided over the meeting, which resolved to submit petitions to the Wuhan Headquarters and the Provincial Government, requesting that the Municipal Government be preserved. More than ten people, including Chen Zubei, were selected as representatives to go to the Wuhan Headquarters and various Party and government agencies to petition. The reasons for their petition are: (1) The city's population is over 200,000, and its direct income accounts for more than half of the city's tax revenue, which is in line with the Municipal Government Organization Law. Therefore, the Municipal Government was approved to be established. (2) The Municipal Government is currently carrying out self-governance, and previous efforts cannot be abandoned. (3) Before the municipal tax was established, the provincial treasury subsidized 40,000 to 50,000 yuan per month. Now the Municipal Government's income is sufficient for self-sufficiency, except for major construction projects. (4) Since its establishment, the Municipal Government has created Zhongshan, Yanjiang, Huanhu, Desheng, and other roads, established the Municipal Bank, and resolved labor-capital disputes, all of which benefit the citizens. (5) Since the establishment of the Municipal Government, the number of municipal elementary schools has increased from several to more than forty. Currently, Mayor Gong has submitted his resignation to the Provincial Government and presented eight major reasons, arguing that the Municipal Government cannot be abolished. After receiving the presentation, Chairman Lu personally consoled Gong. As for whether the Municipal Government will exist or not, it will be decided at the Provincial Affairs Conference. According to political sources, Provincial Government Committee member Xiong Yuxi believes that since the establishment of the Nanchang Municipal Government in January 1927, it has achieved considerable results. Although there are financial difficulties now, one cannot choke on food for fear of choking, so he proposed to the Provincial Affairs Conference to maintain the Municipal Government. However, during this time of intense bandit suppression and financial exhaustion, the two bureaus of Public Works and Finance should be temporarily reorganized into sections to economize. It is reported that this case is likely to be passed.

Difficult Financial Situation of Military and Government Expenses in Hunan Province 107

He Jian Hopes for Central Government Subsidies

Changsha Correspondence: The National Assembly representatives from Hunan Province, including Yin Deyang, departed from Changsha by train on the 28th of last month and traveled to Beijing by ship from Hankou on the 29th. He Jian had printed the Fourth Route Army Military Report and the Hunan Provincial Government Political Work Report and sent personnel to Beijing to deliver them to the representatives, who would then distribute them to key figures in the central government and representatives from various provinces, so that they could understand the situation in Hunan Province. At the same time, he sent a written statement on the difficult financial situation of military and government expenses in Hunan Province to the Hunan representatives, asking them to request the central government to find ways to assist Hunan Province's finances. The difficult financial situation of military and government expenses is recorded as follows:

(A) Military Expenses Situation 108

The Fourth Route Army's expenses were previously stipulated by the central government to be paid from the national tax revenue, but due to regional relations, they were all taken from Hunan Province. Hunan Province's national tax revenue was used for military expenses, and years of turmoil have left the people in deep distress. Moreover, the national tax revenue relies entirely on the salt tax, which is now in a state of stretched to the limit. In the era of the 19th Division in 1929, the monthly expenses were more than 220,000 yuan, and the average monthly income was about 200,000 yuan. In 1930, the Fourth Route Army was formed, with four divisions, two independent brigades, and one garrison commander under its command, requiring monthly expenses of 1.2 million yuan. Currently, with five divisions, one garrison commander, and directly subordinate units, the monthly expenses are 1.5 million yuan. Bandit suppression and temporary expenses are not included. However, in 1930, it was still possible to receive more than 700,000 yuan per month. Since this year, only 400,000 yuan per month has been received, which is not even enough to pay for food and medicine. The difference in salary is very large. As a result, the salaries of officers and soldiers have been in arrears for six months, amounting to more than 3 million yuan. At this time, when bandits and communists are rampant and vigorous suppression is being carried out, it is hoped that proper assistance can be arranged.

(B) Political Expense Situation 109

Since the political situation in Hunan Province roughly stabilized in 1929, the finances have gradually taken shape. It was originally planned to carry out various important policies during the period of political tutelage in order. Unexpectedly, after the Guilin Army entered Hunan in May of last year, the province suffered the disaster of the Red bandits in July 27th, resulting in huge losses to the finances. Therefore, in the second half of 1930, the province's political expenses were increasingly in a state of great financial difficulty. On New Year's Day in January of this year, the salt tax was abolished, resulting in a loss of 600,000 yuan per month in revenue. Although the central government subsidizes 200,000 yuan per month to support the current situation, all the necessary expenses for bandit suppression, troop pensions and rehabilitation, as well as the construction of fortresses, local security, and the salaries of county militias are all allocated from the aforementioned 200,000 yuan subsidy. It is estimated that as of the end of March of this year, the accumulated arrears in political expenses have reached more than 2 million yuan. It was necessary to drastically reduce various expenses. The total amount of reductions in various items is estimated to be 300,000 yuan for party affairs expenses, 180,000 yuan for provincial government expenses, 360,000 yuan for civil affairs expenses, 670,000 yuan for finance expenses, 430,000 yuan for construction expenses, 200,000 yuan for judicial expenses, and 160,000 yuan for office expenses of various agencies, totaling more than 2.29 million yuan in annual reductions. After offsetting income and expenditure, there is still a shortfall of more than 5 million yuan. Therefore, it is hoped that the central government will provide special assistance to maintain the situation. (May 1st)

Hu Shize Talks About His Mission to Russia 111

Departs for Russia from Harbin on May 3rd

Harbin Correspondence: The central government's newly appointed special committee members for the Sino-Soviet Conference, Hu Shize and Qian Tai, and Secretary Lao Weixiu, arrived in Harbin on April 24th. Due to the need to organize their luggage and process their passports, they have delayed their departure until May 3rd, when they will leave the country on the Eurasia train. However, Qian Tai received a telegram from his family on the 28th stating that his father had passed away. After receiving the telegram, Qian telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Beijing, requesting a month's leave. He took a train south on the 28th to return to his hometown in Zhejiang to mourn his father. Therefore, only Hu Shize and Lao Weixiu will leave the country on May 3rd. According to Hu Shize, "Our passports have been processed yesterday and we will certainly depart on May 3rd without delay. After arriving in Russia, I don't know which group of committee members I will be responsible for. The Sino-Soviet Conference will hold its fourth meeting on the 21st of this month, with Ambassador Mo and Karakhan discussing the issue of redeeming the Eastern Railway. Whether the trade and re-establishment of diplomatic relations groups will proceed simultaneously with the Eastern Railway group depends on the situation at the time. However, our diplomatic authorities advocate discussing the Eastern Railway first and then discussing trade and re-establishment of diplomatic relations after it is resolved. Ambassador Mo received clear instructions from the central government when he came to Beijing for instructions. The various issues of the Sino-Soviet Conference are still being carried out according to the established policy. China and Russia share a border of more than 10,000 miles, and the relationship is extremely complex. The conference must be conducted meticulously. Therefore, I expect that it will not be possible to reach a decision within a few months. I have lived in Russia for many years in the past, and I am very willing to go to Russia again to conduct practical studies on Russian affairs during the conference. The trade issue is very important. In the future, it must be carried out with special caution. Because Russia is a state-run business, we must stipulate special measures when signing treaties with them, and we cannot compare them with other free trade countries. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has also drafted several measures and will proceed according to the circumstances. As for the details, the Ministry of Industry is currently drafting them. In the future, the Ministry of Industry may send other personnel to Russia." (April 28th)

Shanxi Newly Revised Two Regulations to Maintain Finance 112

Prohibiting Money Merchants from Delayed Transactions

Restricting the Carrying of Silver Dollars Out of the Border

The Shanxi Provincial Government has recently formulated two measures to maintain finance, namely, prohibiting money merchants from delayed transactions and restricting the carrying of silver dollars out of the border. They have been officially announced. The full text is recorded as follows:

Measures to Suppress Money Shops' Delayed Transactions 113

(1) The money markets of each county and city should determine a fixed location, and report it separately to the county government, the city and county public security bureau, and the chamber of commerce for record. Random gatherings are not allowed. (2) There should be one market per day, fixed from 5:00 AM to 8:00 AM. Afternoon and night markets are all abolished. (3) The daily market hours should be announced by the chamber of commerce. (4) The commission for currency exchange by money shops and stalls is fixed at two cents per yuan, consistent for buying and selling. (5) The county government, the city and county public security bureau, and the chamber of commerce should jointly dispatch personnel to the market every day for supervision. (6) All kinds of remittance must state the following items: 1. Destination of the remittance. 2. Amount. 3. Deadline. 4. Market price. (7) All delayed transactions are prohibited unless there is a legitimate use reported to and approved by the supervisor; violators will be punished. (8) Any business that purchases more than three thousand yuan of silver dollars must report the use and obtain approval from the supervisor before the transaction is allowed; otherwise, it will be considered a violation. (9) Any business that accumulates more than twenty thousand yuan of silver dollars and does not use them within two months will be considered hoarding for speculation. (10) If any money shop violates the provisions of items 7, 8, and 9, once discovered or reported and verified, the following penalties will be imposed: A. Those who secretly engage in delayed transactions will have the transaction canceled and will be fined one times the amount of the transaction for each party. B. Those who purchase more than three thousand yuan of silver dollars without reporting to the supervisor will be fined the same amount as the transaction. C. Those who hoard silver dollars with the intention of speculation will have the entire amount confiscated. D. One-tenth of the fines and confiscations mentioned above will be given to the person who discovered or reported the violation as a reward. (11) If the supervisor deems any remittance or silver dollar transaction made by a money shop to be suspicious, he may, together with the street chief, inspect the shop's books at any time. (12) If other businesses engage in the behavior described in items 7, 8, and 9, they will also be treated as money shops. (13) These measures will take effect from the date of announcement.

Measures for Carrying Silver Dollars Out of the Province with a Permit 114

(1) In order to maintain local finance in this province and prevent the trafficking of silver dollars, specific measures for issuing permits are specially established to facilitate inspection. (2) Anyone carrying more than two hundred yuan of silver dollars out of Shanxi Province must obtain a permit from the provincial government; violators will be treated as traffickers, and in addition to being ordered to stop transportation, they will be punished according to the following items: 1. Two hundred yuan to one thousand yuan: a fine of 10%. 2. One thousand yuan to three thousand yuan: a fine of 20%. 3. Three thousand yuan to ten thousand yuan: a fine of 40%. 4. Twenty thousand yuan to fifty thousand yuan: a fine of 60%. 5. More than fifty thousand yuan: the amount may be confiscated. Two-tenths of the fines mentioned above will be awarded to the original person who discovered the violation, and eight-tenths will be submitted to the Department of Finance for special storage. (3) If a merchant needs to transport silver dollars out of the province to purchase goods, they should, five days in advance, obtain guarantees from two reputable shops, and submit them through the Taiyuan City Chamber of Commerce to the provincial government for verification, or submit them through the county chamber of commerce to the county government for verification, and obtain a permit. The county government should prepare a detailed monthly register of the number of permits issued and submit it to the provincial government for record. (4) When applying for a permit, the reason for using silver dollars, the amount, the names of the shipping company and person, and the name and address of the consignee must be clearly stated for verification. (5) The permit is limited to one use. After delivery, a receipt should be obtained and submitted with the permit to the chamber of commerce for verification, and then forwarded to the issuing authority for cancellation. (6) Anyone who obtains a permit under the false pretense of purchasing goods and is found to be trafficking will have the guarantor jointly penalized. (7) The chamber of commerce is responsible for inspection. If trafficking is suspected, or if the market's silver supply is tight and it is deemed inappropriate to leave the province, the permit may be refused. (8) Each shop or merchant is limited to one permit per application, and no more than three applications may be made within one month. If the number is too high, the government may reduce or suspend the issuance at its discretion. (9) When applying for a permit, stamp duty must be affixed in accordance with the Stamp Tax Law. (10) When silver dollars are carried out of the province, the military police of the railway and the police of the Zhengtai Railway, and the card police and anti-smoking inspection teams of various tax bureaus on land routes are responsible for inspection. (11) When merchants and civilians carry silver dollars out of the province, the military police and bureau cards must verify whether there is a permit and whether the amount matches the permit, and stamp the permit with the seal of the place of inspection to prevent reuse. (12) Silver dollars found without a permit should be sent to the Taiyuan City Public Security Bureau in the province, or to the county governments in the counties, and handled in accordance with these measures. (13) These measures will be implemented from the date of promulgation. All previous regulations prohibiting silver dollars from leaving the province will be repealed.

The Severity of the Chaozhou-Meizhou Flood 115

Losses reach millions or more

Shantou Dispatch: Continuous spring rains in the border area of Fujian, Jiangxi, and Guangdong have caused the Han River to rise sharply. Furthermore, due to the winding downstream tributaries and the accumulation of silt, flooding has occurred. After the 22nd, the weather began to clear. Letters and telegrams from various counties reporting the disaster and requesting relief flooded in. By the 26th, the river had receded. The wooden floodgates at the east gate of Chaoan were removed, and traffic on the Han River gradually resumed. According to a letter from Xingning County, dozens of embankments in the county have collapsed, and many fields and houses have been submerged. More than 20 shops attached to the city have been washed away, dozens of people have been killed or injured, more than ten ships have capsized, and crop losses exceed 100,000. Towns in Meixian County have also been flooded, with water several feet high on flat ground and up to ten feet in low-lying areas. Agricultural losses are also significant. The losses in Sanheba, Gaobei, and Xianghuang in Dapu are particularly severe. On the 19th and 20th, the northern dike of Chaoan County was in the most danger, with the river only two feet away from the dike surface. Leaks occurred multiple times in Qizhushu and the Memorial Pavilion. Fortunately, the Chaoan County Office and the Dike Defense Office, together with local gentry, patrolled day and night, and disaster was averted. The houses in the sixteen villages of the upper and lower Dengrong districts were completely flooded, and the loss of fields, crops, flowers, and fruits was incalculable. In the Jiangdong district, more than ten zhang of the dike base collapsed. The entire Jiangdong and Yixi districts were flooded, and the accumulated water could not be drained. Furthermore, thirty zhang of the dike collapsed at Datangtou Yutingjiao in Qidu. One hundred li of Longxi, Nanggui, and Tuojiang were also submerged. As for Chenghai, the river dike in the Epu district was washed away by four zhang, and the waves rushed directly onto Changqiao Township, turning it into a deep pool. Dozens of villages in the Yuepu and Longxi districts were affected, and the early rice harvest is hopeless. Furthermore, two sections of the Shicuo Long River dike in the Xiabeng district collapsed, totaling about thirteen zhang. Furthermore, between Liyuzhou Beijizhou and Kandong in the Sanjiao dike, more than twenty zhang collapsed, and the water rushed directly into Yuzhou Township, pouring all the way to Shicuo Long Beijilong Fulong Outing Dongdun Jinsha, reaching the outskirts of Shantou. Hundreds of li of rice fields have turned into lakes. The Shantou-Chenghai light rail has completely stopped. The severity of the disaster is unprecedented, and the losses are estimated at millions or more. (27th)

The Tragedy of the Dike Break in Five Embankments in Northern Jiangsu 116

More than ten thousand mu of embanked fields are submerged

Yangzhou Dispatch: This year's Yangtze River tide is exceptionally high. In addition, the southeast wind has been strong in recent days, and the river tide has directly impacted the north bank, making the situation even more severe. At 9:00 AM today, the river dike between the five embankments and the four embankments on the opposite bank of Zhenjiang suddenly collapsed. In an instant, the area from the riverbank to Hongqiao Town became a watery land. The submerged area is more than five square li, and the submerged fields and crops are about ten thousand mu. About two thousand houses and countless livestock were affected. Fortunately, the breach occurred during the day, and many people climbed onto trees, so there were few deaths. There are more households in the western part of the embankment than in the eastern part. Fortunately, there is a long-distance highway in between, and the water did not flood in; otherwise, the losses would have been even greater. It is reported that various charitable authorities in Yangzhou and Zhenjiang, led by the Red Swastika Society, have purchased dry food and mobilized river boats to provide free crossings and rush to the disaster area to provide emergency relief and rescue the victims. However, the sky is still overcast, and the wind is increasing. It is still unknown whether other dikes will continue to collapse. (4th)

Murderer from Shanghai Escorted to Suzhou 120

Zhu Linru, who lived near Disingway Road in Shanghai, had a wife named Jiang, who was intimate with Shen Junying, a partner in Zhang Shaoqing's lumber company. Li of Hefei purchased 73 mu of land at the foot of Xiaowang Mountain in Suzhou Township to build a large tomb for Li Jingxi, the former Prime Minister. Unexpectedly, land dealers stole and sold the ancestral tombs of the Wu Lin Yu and other families on the land to Li, and after destroying and excavating the tombs, they abandoned the remains. Wuxi

Continued Negotiation and Signing of a Labor-Management Agreement in Silk Factories 123

The issue of labor-management agreement in silk factories in this county has been resolved after the Party and government authorities invited both labor and management to the county government to fairly mediate and continue to sign a labor-management agreement. A formal notice has now been issued, and it will be implemented as scheduled. The revised labor-management agreement is recorded as follows: (1) Wages: The highest wage is set at 57 cents. (2) Bonuses: Bonuses will be paid on the 3rd of each month. (Deduction method: Half a day's work deducted for half a day's absence; one day's work deducted for one day's absence; one and a half day's work deducted for one and a half day's absence, and so on. The bonus method will still be handled according to the original arbitration method.) If the silk price rises beyond 1,000 taels, the bonus will be changed to four days per month, and the deduction method will revert to the old method. (3) Holidays: The original holidays were set for the 1st and 16th of each month. If there is a commemorative day in the month, the holiday can be moved to the commemorative day. If the factory needs to unwind silk, the holiday may also be moved, but the factory should notify the district labor union and report to the labor union in advance. (4) Salaries: The salaries of employees that were reduced by 10% after the previous arbitration will be restored to their original state. (5) Silkworm moths: The price of silkworm moths for employees will be 45 cents uniformly. (6) The effective period of this agreement is from May 1, 1931, to December 31, 1932. (7) Commemorative days: Work will be suspended uniformly on commemorative days in accordance with central regulations. The method of payment will be determined separately. (8) This agreement will be effective immediately after both parties sign it.

Establishment of a Model Irrigation Area by the Construction Committee 124

Since the Central Construction Committee was ordered by the National Government to handle irrigation projects, especially since agricultural production in our country is lagging behind, it is necessary to plan model irrigation projects separately to promote and revitalize agriculture. It has petitioned the National Government to organize a National Model Irrigation Administration, and the Legislative Yuan has approved the organizational regulations. Therefore, it will first establish a model irrigation area office in Wujin and Wuxi to carry out electric irrigation. All of the 50,000+ mu of irrigation fields of the Qishuyan Power Plant and the former First Irrigation Area Committee will be handed over to the office for management. Sun Fushi has been appointed as the director of the office, Jiang Zhan as the deputy director, and Tan Youcen as the engineer and head of both the engineering and general affairs sections. The organization was established at the end of last month and notified various agencies for their information. It is reported that the office is trying to improve the management of existing irrigation fields and projects in order to increase efficiency, and is also actively planning expansion projects.

Nantong

Sea Bandits and Salt Smugglers in Tong Region Eliminated 135

The sea bandits and salt smugglers in the various fields of the Tong region in northern Jiangsu have been eliminated after days of suppression by the fishing protection water and land army and police. However, there are still more than ten bandit ships drifting in the Fengjue ocean area. The military police have rushed to pursue and suppress them.

The Issue of the Waterway on the Yangtze River at Langshan 136

After a joint survey by the Ministry of Communications, the Central Construction Committee, and the Naval Hydrographic Bureau, it was determined that if Langshan were to collapse into the river, it would be more difficult to straighten the waterway in the river. Li Shengbo, the representative of this county to the National Assembly, has consulted with representatives of various counties in Jiangsu Province and proposed to straighten it.

Hall Order for the Public Security Bureau to Dismiss the Police Team 137

The Department of Civil Affairs ordered the county government to inform the Public Security Bureau that there was no need to have a police team and that it should be dismissed immediately. The police soldiers should be changed to ordinary patrol police and serve in accordance with the regulations.

Women's Overall Championship...Yangzhou Middle School Girls won

The 4th Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Joint Sports Meet ended successfully yesterday. The overall championship of the competition was won by Provincial Nanjing Middle School, and the women's overall championship was won by Yangzhou Middle School Girls. Provincial Shanghai Middle School won the men's basketball championship, and Provincial Suzhou Middle School won the men's field events championship. In the women's group, Yangzhou Middle School Girls won the track and field championship, Suzhou Girls' Middle School won the basketball championship, and Su Zhenhua Girls' School won the volleyball championship. Provincial Nanjing Girls' Middle School won the tennis championship. The closing ceremony was held at 5:00 PM, and the awards were presented by Madam Zhao Lingxian, wife of Chen Hexian. The details are recorded below.

Men's Soccer Final: Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing Middle School Wins Championship 140

One to Zero Victory over Jiangsu Provincial Suzhou Middle School

(Yesterday, the 4th) At 1:00 PM, the soccer final between Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing Middle School and Jiangsu Provincial Suzhou Middle School took place. The result was one to zero, with Nanjing Middle School winning the championship. The referee was Tang Zhongguang, and the linesmen were He Chunhui and Chen Jixiang.

The Weather Turns Unfavorable

At that time, the sky was covered with dark clouds, and the wind was very strong. As soon as the game started, the rain poured down. The soccer skills of both schools are among the best in the province. Despite the unfavorable weather, the game was quite lively.

Taking Advantage of the Wind, Missing Opportunities

After selecting the venue and starting the game, Suzhou Middle School had the advantage of the tailwind, making it easier to attack. Nanjing Middle School, facing the headwind, found it difficult to send the ball into the opponent's zone. Sometimes, the wind blew the ball back, creating dangerous situations. Suzhou Middle School had several scoring opportunities, but they all missed them. Nanjing Middle School tried to defend and withstand the critical situation.

Switching Sides to Fight Again

Nanjing Middle School survived the difficult period without any mistakes. Everyone celebrated. After switching sides, Nanjing Middle School took advantage of the tailwind and switched from defense to offense. The ball often lingered in Suzhou Middle School's zone. Lu Yaxiong, a famous sprinter from Suzhou Middle School, switched from center back to inside defender and repeatedly saved dangerous balls. His contributions were significant.

Touching the Post and Going into the Net

About twenty minutes into the game, neither side had scored. Chen Hongqi, the right forward of Nanjing Middle School, shot fiercely at the goal from about ten yards in front of Suzhou's goal. Xu Yuwen tried to push the ball out of bounds with both hands. Who knew that it would hit the goalpost and bounce strongly into the net?

Trying to Counterattack

After Suzhou Middle School conceded a goal, all the players were motivated and tried to counterattack in order to win the championship. Their left and right wings had two excellent crosses with perfect landing points. Unfortunately, the forwards moved too slowly and missed the opportunities. Moreover, the heavy rain continued, the field was muddy, and the ball became heavier due to the water, making it extremely difficult to play.

The Whistle Blows to End the Game

At exactly 3:00 PM, the time was up, and the referee blew the whistle to end the game. Suzhou Middle School unfortunately suffered a crushing defeat by one to zero. Nanjing Middle School also won the tournament's soccer championship with this precious goal. The team lineups for both teams are as follows:

(1) Deng Rongling (Nanjing Middle School) defeated Wang Jiayou (Nantong Middle School)

Six to Three, Six to Three

(2) Zhu Huanjiu (Nanjing Middle School) defeated Mao Fukui (Nantong Middle School)

Six to Four, Four to Six, Six to Two

Nanjing Middle School has almost always won the tournament tennis championship in the past. Last year, Dongwu University participated in the amateur competition, and facing strong opponents, they suffered a crushing defeat. This year, they had a smooth journey, did not encounter any opponents, and won the championship easily.

[Image: Viewing the Nanjing Middle School team that won the men's volleyball championship (photographed by this newspaper)]

In yesterday's match, Deng and Zhu, the two players from Nanjing Middle School, both won by being steady, combining powerful and skillful shots, and never overdoing it. Wang and Mao, the two players from Nantong Middle School, were also skilled, but Wang's serve was weak and was repeatedly taken advantage of by Deng. Zhu vs. Mao

Since Nanjing Middle School won both singles matches, the championship was in their hands. The doubles match in the afternoon was not held.

Two to Zero Victory over Shanghai Middle School

The boys' volleyball team of Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing Middle School won the championship by defeating the boys' volleyball team of Shanghai Provincial Shanghai Middle School in two consecutive games. In the first game, Nanjing Middle School's momentum did not diminish, and they won repeatedly. The score in the first half was still eleven to seven. The final score was twenty-one to fourteen. Nanjing Middle School won two consecutive games and won the championship. Nanjing Middle School's volleyball skills are more mature, their attacks are powerful, and their setting and spiking are also skillful. Shanghai Middle School seems to be inferior. However, the south wind was very strong yesterday, making it difficult to play volleyball. Both offense and defense had to be careful at all times.

Two to Zero Victory over Yangzhou Middle School for Girls

Women's Volleyball Final: Suzhou Zhenhua Wins Championship 144

Two to One Victory over Jingzhi

In the women's volleyball final yesterday, Suzhou Zhenhua Girls' School defeated Wuxi Jingzhi Girls' School by two to one and won the championship. Jingzhi won first and then lost, while Zhenhua became more and more courageous. The performance was excellent. The referee was Huang Wenjian.

The Wind Was Strong and the Ball Flew

The south wind was very strong yesterday, and the volleyball was light, so it flew with the wind. It was even more difficult to serve against the wind, especially in women's volleyball. Therefore, the side with the tailwind won yesterday.

A Glimpse of the Volleyball Skills

Zhenhua's performance was excellent yesterday. They did not panic after losing first, which was the reason for their victory. In particular, the volleyball skills of Tang Lianjuan, the center back in the first row, were stable and commendable, and she was the most outstanding. Yang Luyi in the second row was also strong. The credit for the championship lies in the cooperation of the entire team. Jingzhi was inferior yesterday and made mistakes from time to time. However, Ni Yunshang and Zhu Huiyang were indeed excellent women's volleyball players.

Taking Advantage of the Wind to Attack

As the whistle blew to start the game, Jingzhi attacked first with the tailwind. The ball shuttled back and forth over the net. Lu Yingya from Jingzhi set the ball, but it went too far out of bounds. Zhenhua scored the first point and took the lead. Ge Fuming from Zhenhua returned the attack, and Jingzhi also killed the ball, tying the score at one all. Both teams played carefully, and Jingzhi took the lead with a score of eight to six and continued to score. In the first half of the first game, Jingzhi won with a score of eleven to seven.

Trying Hard to Counterattack

After Zhenhua failed in the first game, they were determined and extraordinarily cautious. The wind was also favorable. After a score of eight to five, they won successively, winning the first half of the game with a score of eleven to five. Jingzhi gradually showed panic and made mistakes from time to time, while Zhenhua's connection was excellent, especially Tang Lianjuan, the center back in the first row, who was the most outstanding. Her counterattacks and smashes were perfect. As a result, they won back one game with a score of twenty-one to fifteen, tying the score at one to one. Everyone was delighted.

The Outcome Was Decided in the Third Game

The outcome was decided in the third game. The atmosphere was tense, and shouts rose from time to time. Beautiful songs were frequently sent to the ears. Jingzhi initially seemed to have the upper hand. Zhang Zhiyuan served and took the lead with a score of eight to six. However, Yang Luyi also scored two points, tying the score at eight all. Jingzhi had the tailwind. In the first half of the game, they took the lead with a score of eleven to eight. After switching sides, the competition between the two teams was extremely fierce. The score difference was only one or two points, and even reached eighteen all. Then, at nineteen to nineteen, Jingzhi made another mistake, letting each other make mistakes, and ultimately failed. The score was twenty-one to nineteen. As a result, Zhenhua won the championship with joy, with a score of two to one.

Yesterday's Victory over Songjiang Girls' Middle School

Twenty-Six to Twenty-Two

Suzhou Girls' Middle School won the women's basketball championship. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, they defeated Songjiang Girls' Middle School by twenty-six to twenty-two in the final. The referee was Shao Ji.

Two Excellent Athletes

Before describing the match, Guan Yi first introduced two excellent athletes, namely Zhang Yingfen, the center of Suzhou Girls' Middle School, and Xu Jinzhu, the center of Songjiang Girls' Middle School. They were quick on their feet, ran fast, and threw accurately. They could also command. Miss Zhang was even better. Her throws were always accurate. Yesterday, she scored twenty-two points out of the team's total of twenty-six points. Miss Xu was closely guarded by Wang Liangyu, making it difficult for her to move freely. She looked very disappointed.

The Skills of the Two Teams

The forwards of Suzhou Girls' Middle School cooperated very well and showed great skill. They were worthy of being the championship team. The guards Wang and Yao did not let their guard down at all and were also contributors. The forwards of Songjiang Girls' Middle School were also good, but their guards were weaker. However, Zhang Yingfen was definitely not someone who could be guarded by ordinary people. Both teams often charged forward with the ball and did not know how to turn around when blocked. This was a major problem that should be corrected.

The Match Situation

After Zhang Yingfen of Suzhou Girls' Middle School opened the scoring, they won successively, scoring seven points. Xu Jinzhu of Songjiang Girls' Middle School then opened the scoring. Suzhou Girls' Middle School took the lead all the way. The score at halftime was seventeen to eight. In the last eight minutes, Songjiang Girls' Middle School tried their best to counterattack and came closer, but ultimately failed.

Celebrating Victory

After Nanjing Middle School won the volleyball and tennis finals, they won two championships and cheered with joy. All the athletes paraded around the field with firecrackers and school flags, and the cheers were thunderous. The losers were so angry that they were silent. Not rejoicing in victory and not worrying about defeat, this kind of cultivation is rare. However, the courage of the benevolent is something that cannot be ignored.

Peddlers Wandering Around

Yesterday, the sky was cloudy, and the southeast wind was strong. There were only ball games in the morning, and not many spectators came to the venue. It rained again in the afternoon. The business of ordinary peddlers was several times better in the previous three days. Yesterday, they suffered a big loss. In particular, those selling fruit had no customers. The sound of people shouting "sugarcane" and "bananas" could be heard everywhere.

Gifts from This Newspaper

This newspaper specially prepared two large flags for this tournament and gave them to the men's field championship team and the women's track and field championship team. They were now won by Suzhou Middle School and Yangzhou Middle School for Girls.

Welcome Special Books

The "Soccer Training Method," "Soccer Rule Questions and Answers," and "Basketball Training Method," newly published by the Diligent Bookstore at No. 39 Xinmin Village, Malang Road, Shanghai, were written by Wu Bangwei, the director general of the tournament. The content is rich and popular throughout the country. Male and female athletes are very welcome. The bookstore donated the soccer championship flag, which was won by Nanjing Middle School yesterday.

Free Talk: World Small Events

By Haike

The Edmonton Council in London proposed to name the trees planted in many secondary streets after famous scientists as a form of memorial.

Britain plans to build a small airplane that can seat two people. When folded, it will only be eight feet wide, eight feet eleven inches high, and twenty-two feet five inches long. It is planned to be placed in submarines for use after it is built.

According to a well-known European health expert, a sixteen-year-old should eat the same amount of food as a strong man engaged in outdoor work such as gardening in order to be strong.

The development of the electrical industry in Britain far exceeds that of six years ago. People use twice as much electricity as they did six years ago.

Switzerland's scenery is the best in the world. Every year, many people go there for sightseeing. Therefore, there are 3,600 hotels, employing 61,000 people, with a total capital of 60 million pounds.

Britain has rabbit farms dedicated to raising rabbits. The annual yield of rabbit skins is 150,000 pieces.

The number of female criminals in New York is increasing day by day. According to the statistics of female prisoners in various prisons in 1920, there were only 1,150 people. Now, it has more than doubled.

Neighbor's Sigh

By Ke Dingan

The theory of equality between men's rights and women's rights has been widely discussed recently. However, it is merely a hollow claim without any practical implementation. A certain Mr. Jia next door works for the local electric power company. His wife, Ms. Mou, is known for her virtue. They have one son and one daughter. The son is five years old and the daughter is three years old. Usually, the relationship between the couple is very harmonious. On holidays, they often go out together, talking and laughing, and their happiness knows no bounds. People in the same neighborhood admire their affection and happiness. Unexpected events often occur that others cannot predict, and I will now describe one of them.

In recent months, Mr. Jia has suddenly changed his normal behavior. Usually, he would return home at 5:00 PM every day after finishing work at the company to enjoy family time. His wife would prepare meals with great care and diligence. This is indeed a happy thing in life. However, in recent months, Mr. Jia has often not returned home late at night, and even when he did return, it was at the crack of dawn. He also often quarreled with his wife over trivial matters. She still feared that he was being mistreated outside, so she swallowed her anger and resentment and spoke kindly in an attempt to restore their original harmony. Unexpectedly, she incurred his anger, abuse, and wild cursing. She endured it and remained silent. This went on for many days. She suddenly heard people say that her husband had found someone else outside. She was saddened when she heard this, but did not deeply believe it at first. However, considering the situation, it seemed to be true. If he cherished the new and abandoned the old, then she would be alone and helpless. What would she rely on for her future life? Worries piled up, and she became very haggard.

One day, a green-clad postman delivered a letter. Her name was written on the envelope. It was received by her mother-in-law, who also knew a little about her. Knowing that it was written by a man, she secretly kept it and did not give it to her. She waited for Mr. Jia to return and secretly read it with him. As expected, it was sent by another man to his wife. Mr. Jia was extremely angry. He secretly regretted that he had no grounds to pursue the matter. Now that he had this letter, he could get his wish. While Mr. Jia and his mother were reading the letter, she was preparing the meal, not knowing anything about it at first. Mr. Jia quickly rushed into the kitchen, grabbed his wife's hair, dragged her out, and punched and kicked her. Her mother-in-law stood by and watched, adding fuel to the fire. When Mr. Jia was exhausted, he finally stopped. His wife was exhausted and hoarse, lying on the ground and unable to get up. She still did not know how she had offended her husband. While she was thinking, Mr. Jia threw the letter on the ground and said, "No wonder your attitude has been so strange recently. So that's what's going on." Then he laughed coldly. She looked at the letter and knew that it was sent by a boyfriend from before she was married. The letter was just a greeting and did not involve any obscene content. The reason for his offense was because of this. However, she had no strength to defend herself. After that, Mr. Jia confined her to a room. I often heard her crying softly when I woke up in the middle of the night. Her voice was so sad that I couldn't bear to listen. My room is relatively close to hers, so I heard it very sadly. In civilized Shanghai, this is what is meant by equality between men and women. Alas.

How to Enhance Marital Bliss

By Chen Yuanliang

Marital bliss is the key to lifelong happiness. Otherwise, even if they appear to be compatible, they are actually alienated. Even if they have not officially separated, they are forced to live together, which is completely devoid of joy. People in Europe and America have extensively studied the issue of marriage. Recently, I read an article written by a certain gentleman in the Japanese magazine "Women's World" in Tokyo. I feel that he is very considerate and his words are very pertinent. I have translated it as follows:

The author believes that the organization of a family is purely based on love. If you can diligently care for it, love can be maintained. The rules to be followed by husbands are divided into eleven items, roughly divided into habits, jealousy, finance, holidays, health, clothing, diet, children, and household affairs. The following are several items that husbands should not do:

(1) Do not let cigarette ashes fall on the floor when you are relaxing at home. (Japanese people sit on the floor.) This will cause your wife to have to do more work.

(2) Treat each other like guests. Respect each other for a long time. Do not immediately undress during meals because you are afraid of the heat.

(3) Do not immediately complain to her if you feel unwell or slightly uncomfortable. She is already tired enough from managing the household.

(4) Do not use unclean handkerchiefs in front of others. This will cause others to despise her occasional negligence.

(5) Avoid boredom in ordinary life. You should often tell stories and interesting anecdotes to make her laugh.

(6) When her face is charming, you should praise her beauty. If she looks unhappy, you should be even more gentle and comforting.

(7) Those who criticize their wives in front of others because their ties are not changed or their shoes are not polished will never have a perfect family.

(8) Even if you are reluctant, you must accompany her to the mall when she wants you to. On the way back, you can go to a cafe together for tea and a rest.

(9) You must seek her opinion on everything. Although her opinion may not be correct, it is not necessarily wrong.

(10) Men who are married should not be too reserved. Otherwise, they will be like wood and stone, and there will be no interest in them.

(11) Love should be expressed. You should frankly call her "my love" or "I love you." Since you have been married for a long time, you don't need to be shy like on the night of your honeymoon.

(12) There are roughly two types of female beauty: healthy beauty and spiritual beauty. If your wife possesses one of these two, you should try your best to praise her characteristics so that she knows that you have already appreciated her true interest.

(13) If you feel bad, you should remain calm and not get angry easily. You should especially avoid the bad habits of slamming bowls and hitting tables.

(14) You should often be close to your wife's family. Do not prevent her from returning to her parents' home. When you meet again after a short separation, it will increase the taste of love. However, love is best when it lasts for a long time. Use it sparingly. If it is too strong during the honeymoon, it will inevitably decline after a long time.

(15) Do not boast about your income in front of your wife. Do not miss the opportunity. Do not lie. Do not forget her birthday. You should celebrate it to commemorate it.

(16) If you find that a button is missing and not sewn on her clothes, do not immediately say harsh words, which may cause misunderstandings.

(17) When questioning your wife, do not raise your voice. Prevent neighbors, servants, and children from knowing about it. It is related to her dignity.

(18) Do not say in front of your children that they would starve to death without you. You must have fun with them so that they always have a lovable father in their hearts.

(19) You should introduce your female friends when you meet them on the road. Otherwise, it will easily arouse suspicion and cause jealousy.

(20) You should explain the meaning of how difficult it is to earn money and how easy it is to spend it. Advise her to save money. Explore its use, but do not act like a miser.

(21) Do not move the furniture in the house without permission. It will disrupt its order.

(22) If you are not satisfied with the clothes your wife makes, you should not criticize them as much as possible. You should forgive her for having exhausted her efforts.

(23) If you are away from home for a short time, you should frequently send letters to report on your trip. Although the price of a small postcard is not much, your wife will be able to break the lonely air of the boudoir when she sees the words "you are safe."

Mei's Southern News

By Zhi

Mei Wan Hua and his party were recently invited to perform in Hong Kong and Guangdong. They will use their latest research results to consult with people in the south. They have already been reported to have traveled south from Shanghai. Here is a summary of their activities after arriving in Guangdong for the information of those who are interested.

On the 20th, the Taiyo Maru arrived in Hong Kong. On the 22nd, they transferred from Macau to Zhongshan County and visited Mr. Tang Shaochuan. They had a long conversation and went to Cuiheng Village to visit Mr. Sun Yat-sen's former residence and laid a wreath. On the 23rd, they returned to Macau and accompanied Minister Liu Yulin to the Governor of Macau's tea party. At 2:30 PM on the 25th, they arrived in Guangzhou by the Foshan round. Many people came to the round to welcome them. Deng Sixiao, the personal secretary of Chairman Chen, represented the welcome and shook hands with Wan Hua. After landing, Chairman Chen and Commander-in-Chief Chen hosted a banquet at Tuisi Garden. When they landed, thousands of people watched.

After Wan landed, he attended a welcome party at the East Asia Hotel. This party was jointly organized by the Bahe Guild Hall, the Lawyers' Association, the Nanyang Tobacco Company, and the Haizhu Theater. Mr. Tao Junan accompanied them. The representative of the Lawyers' Association delivered a welcome speech. Wan gave a reply speech, which was translated into Cantonese by Mr. Tao Jun. The guests applauded.

After leaving the welcome party, they went to visit Chairman Chen at his private residence and had a long conversation. They continued to visit Commander-in-Chief Chen, but he was going to Yantang to review the troops and did not have time to meet. At 6:00 PM, they attended Tuisi Garden. Wan Hua wore a night dress. The guests and hosts were happy. Commander-in-Chief Chen also sent a large horizontal plaque.

The first performance was on the 29th. The headquarters reserved many seats, all vying to enjoy the artistic drama of China. The first night was Xi Shi, the second night was The Legend of Taizhen, the third night was Farewell My Concubine, the fourth night was The Legend of Taizhen, the fifth night was Farewell My Concubine, and the sixth night was Luo Shen. This was the scheduled repertoire, which was also requested by various circles in Guangdong.

Indian Travel Notes (43)

By Linghua

On the 27th, the Krishna Society invited me to dinner. This temple is very large, about half a mile. The buildings are Western-style and very clean. There are 200 monks and they also support the poor. Men and women work. The food is very rich, about 20 dishes. The Indian cuisine is also no worse than Chinese food. Some tastes may be better than Chinese food, but they are very different. The Indian way of eating is different from Chinese food. The so-called 20 dishes are eaten by one person, divided and not shared. Half of it is similar to Western food. When I eat at Indian people's places, I pay attention to how much I eat. If one person eats 120 dishes, it is only a waste of resources. What are they? Indian people have strange customs. All food that has been eaten by others, no matter how much, is discarded. You are not allowed to eat other people's food. It has become a religious superstition. You don't drink people's tea, and people are not allowed to drink it. You don't touch people. The reason is due to the class system. I still don't understand the rules of communication. In short, there are many conditions for giving people food. There are also many conditions for people to eat with them. It makes our heads dizzy. If someone accidentally drinks someone else's tea, or gives people tea and food, or eats with others, they violate the rules. Therefore, when Gandhi went to England to study, his family punished him because he had to eat with the British. It is also a violation of the rules to marry a foreigner. The obstacles are indescribable.

As for the taste of the food, it is purely vegetarian, with many fragrant flowers, sweet and crispy foods, and milk. Milk has many variations, about 20 kinds. All five original substances of milk, sugar, oil, flowers, and fruits are common foods for Indian people. There are flowers in all seasons, and fruits and vegetables are fragrant. Therefore, the vegetarian food tastes very good. However, the sweetness is too great, and we cannot eat the Indian bananas. Today, the world's food taste evaluation is still the Chinese as the first. However, I think that the good Indian food is definitely no worse than Chinese food. As for Indian food, lunch is rice and dinner is noodles, which is the norm. I will give a lecture at the Theosophical Society. The Krishna Society is typing my lecture manuscript with a typewriter. Their monks generally use English. This Indian church is all over India, and also in Europe and America. As for their funds, they are all donated from the United States. Without the United States, there would be no sponsors in the world today.

On the 28th, at 6:00 PM, I gave a lecture at the Theosophical Society. Mr. Wu Tingfang, a late friend, was once a member of this society. It exists in all countries around the world. The president is a woman. Dr. Besant is 84 years old this year. She has founded many universities and charities. Some say that she has supernatural powers, but I don't know. The topic of the lecture was why children cry, it is because they miss their mothers. There were four or five hundred listeners. Some held oil and wiped my head, which is an Indian custom. The main purpose of my lecture was the world's anti-war movement. Motherhood must be used. The result was to achieve Sun Yat-sen's Datong Doctrine. All the British and Indian newspapers published the lecture manuscript that night. It will be published in the society's January report, saying that it will reach 47 countries around the world. There are hundreds of local branches in India. In this society, I met many men and women from all over the world. The farthest ones were from Australia and New Zealand. There were also people from various Islamic countries, which was very rare.

Huo Sang's Detective Case in Rotary Club Story Collection: Turning Point (4)

By Cheng Xiaoqing

(2) Inexplicable

Just then, I suddenly felt a light tap on my left shoulder. At the same time, a fragrance hit my nostrils. I immediately stopped and turned my head, face to face with that friend in a suit. I didn't know him, nor did I know what he meant. I was about to ask a question when the man suddenly made an unexpected move. His right hand reached into his outer jacket pocket and shoved something white into my left hand. Then he released his foot and hurried forward.

I was stunned for a moment. Originally, this move completely exceeded my expectations. Although my right hand had touched the gun handle, it was inconvenient to fire it randomly. Because I didn't know what was in my left hand. My fingers naturally squeezed it, but it was a small white towel. In this squeezing movement, there were still some subtle rubbing sounds. Strange. What is this? The small bag was not heavy and didn't look like a dangerous item. At this time, my reason instructed me. The first step should be to see what was in the bag. So my right hand immediately released the gun handle and quickly opened the bag. It was a fine white gauze scarf with folded edges all around. It had been ironed and had a strong fragrance. Fortunately, this small bag was rolled up and not knotted. I had already unfolded it in two or three seconds. But after unfolding it, my eyes came into contact with the contents of the bag, and this shock was extraordinary. It turned out that the white towel contained a string of brightly glittering pearl necklaces.

I seemed to have entered a dream. A surprised exclamation came out of my throat automatically. The cigarette in my mouth also fell to the ground at once. I seemed to

Grand Closing Ceremony 146

Mrs. Chen Hexian Awards Prizes

At 4:00 PM on the fourth day, the grand closing ceremony was held. All schools lined up in front of the command post. Mr. Chen Hexian, the vice president of the conference, delivered the closing remarks, stating that the various achievements of this session were better compared to previous sessions, and many new records were discovered. This was the result of the hard work of all students, as well as the attention of various schools to sports and the promotion of society. He hoped for even better results next year, and also hoped that those who won national championships would not be complacent and should continue to work hard, not only to win national championships, but also to compete on the world sports stage. He told those who did not win championships not to be discouraged, as failure is the mother of success. As long as they work hard, it will not be difficult to win championships next year. Then, the General Secretary Wu Bangwei reported the results of various competitions, saying that the results were greatly affected by the wind during the conference, but we acknowledge that the results of this session are very good, and the sportsmanship of the athletes is also very good. There were never any disputes in the various competitions of this session. He hoped that next year there would be better results than this year. Finally, Mrs. Zhao Lingxian, the wife of Chen Hexian, awarded the prizes. The male overall championship winner received a large silver trophy from Zhang Xueliang's Executive Yuan, etc. The female overall championship winner received a flag and silver shield from President Chiang Kai-shek and Director Chen, etc. The field event championship winner received a silver shield from He Yingqin, Dai Chuanxian, etc. The track event championship winner received a silver shield from the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Interior, etc. The winners of the various ball game championships and the track and field events were awarded silver shields, prize flags, "The Complete Works of Sun Yat-sen," and medals. There were four types of medals: gold medals for first place, silver medals for second place, bronze medals for third place, and copper medals for fourth place.

Competition in Wind and Rain 147

Yesterday was the fourth day of the conference. The southeast wind was even stronger, and the sky was covered with dark clouds, unlike the bright and beautiful scenes of the previous days. The wind was wild and the ground was vast, making the dust even more noticeable. There were not many scattered spectators at the two venues yesterday morning. As the afternoon progressed, the wind grew stronger, the clouds grew thicker, and there was a hint of rain. Sure enough, the ball field was not opened in the afternoon, and rain began to fall from the sky. The atmosphere in the field became even more tense. In the afternoon, basketball and football were played entirely in the heavy rain. Ball games were already difficult due to the wind, and the rain made it even more difficult for the athletes to fight. Only a few spectators were present, which was a bit disappointing. At 3:00 PM, the ball games ended, and the military band played triumphant music as everyone returned. Vice President Chen was very enthusiastic about promoting sports. Despite the strong wind, he still went to the venue with his wife and son to watch. He stood briefly at the ball field and expressed his admiration for the spirit of the players at the most exciting moments. Field Director Wu, Chief Referee Zhang, and Ms. Yu Qingtang were busy distributing the prizes, and it seemed that they were also very hesitant in weighing the importance of each prize.

Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing High School won the men's team championship at the conference. There were a total of six championships in the men's division, and Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing High School won four, including track, football, volleyball, and tennis, which was very rare and a new record for the conference. At the closing ceremony, firecrackers were set off and military music was played to celebrate their victory.

Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou High School for Girls won the women's team overall championship at the conference. The four championships in the women's division were divided among four schools, each winning one. However, Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou High School for Girls won the track and field championship, so they won the overall championship.

Changes in Women's Overall Championship 150

It is a pity that Suzhou Girls' High School lost

The women's team overall championship has now been won by Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou High School for Girls, because they won the track and field competition. However, there was a slight change in the process. I will record it to observe the shift in the situation.

A Small Misunderstanding 151

During the semi-finals the day before, the women's volleyball game was between Suzhou Girls' High School and Jingzhi Girls' School, and the women's basketball game was between Suzhou Girls' High School and Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai High School for Girls. Both were held at 9:00 AM at the same time. The players of Suzhou Girls' High School all had two roles, playing both volleyball and basketball. Therefore, the leaders of Suzhou Girls' High School and Jingzhi Girls' School discussed the day before to hold the volleyball game one hour earlier. However, Jingzhi insisted on holding it at the original time of 9:00 AM, and Shanghai High School for Girls also refused to reschedule the basketball game. Suzhou Girls' High School had no choice but to supplement the two teams with track and field players.

Divided Attention 152

Suzhou Girls' High School was distracted, paying attention to both, and seemed flustered, with the difficulty of not knowing which to follow. They decided to try volleyball first. Zhang Yingfen, a basketball star, played volleyball, but was still thinking about basketball, and her will was not focused, so they lost to Jingzhi. Fortunately, after the volleyball game, she rushed to the rescue and reorganized her team, so they were not defeated.

Clash of Strengths 153

Zhen defeated Jingzhi, but Suzhou Zhenhua's results were worse than Suzhou Girls' High School, so Suzhou Girls' High School had the possibility of defeating Jingzhi. If they defeated Jingzhi, then the volleyball championship would be in their hands.

Championship Transfer 154

If the volleyball championship was won by Suzhou Girls' High School, then with the women's basketball championship, the overall championship would also belong to them. Now, because of a misunderstanding, the overall situation has shifted, which is a pity for Suzhou Girls' High School.

Excellent Sportsmanship 155

The sportsmanship at the conference on the fourth day was excellent. The winners were not arrogant, and the losers were not discouraged. During the ball games, both the winning and losing teams cheered, and they did not take the championship as the ultimate goal. On the third day, the semi-final ball games had conflicting times, but they were able to sacrifice everything to ensure the smooth progress of the conference, which is especially commendable. The fourth runner of the Suzhou Girls' High School team, the women's 400-meter relay champion, Zhang Maolan, was stepped on by someone's shoe spikes, and blood flowed like a stream, but she still rushed forward and won first place. This kind of spirit must be recorded to tell all athletes.

Today is the anniversary of the Chinese Kuomintang leader's inauguration as the Extraordinary Grand President in Guangzhou in the tenth year of the Republic of China (i.e., the anniversary of the establishment of the Revolutionary Government), and it also coincides with the opening of the National Assembly. The Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters has scheduled a celebration and commemorative meeting today at 9:00 AM, gathering representatives from various agencies, organizations, schools, and party headquarters at all levels, at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce at Tianhougong Bridge. Japanese Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu Kui, accompanied by secretaries Hayashi and Horiuchi, will take the 11:45 PM express train to Beijing tonight to meet with Foreign Minister Wang and continue talks on Sino-Japanese legal rights negotiations, and to conclude the issue of compensation for the Nanjing and Hankou incidents.
