After the Breakdown of Sino-British and Sino-French Legal Rights Negotiations 165

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Issued a Statement Yesterday

The Municipal Party Headquarters Advocates Automatic Abolition

According to news from diplomatic circles in this city, Sino-British legal rights negotiations broke down because the British insisted on maintaining consular jurisdiction for ten years in the ten-mile area centered on the customs in the four commercial ports of Shanghai, Tianjin, Hankou, and Guangzhou. Because the United Kingdom, the United States, and France were not sincere in the legal rights negotiations, our side issued two statements yesterday afternoon to announce to Chinese and foreign people the process of the legal rights negotiations and the issue of responsibility for the breakdown. However, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs office in Shanghai did not issue any documents on this matter because the information office had already been abolished. However, the Municipal Party Headquarters will have a proposal, which is to request the National Assembly to order the National Government to automatically announce the abolition of all unequal treaties regarding legal rights. It is said that this proposal will be submitted to the Shanghai All Sectors Celebration of the National Assembly Opening Congress held at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce this morning for approval, and then telegraphed to the Nanjing National Assembly for discussion and implementation.

According to a Reuters report from Shanghai on the 4th, the fourth point in the four points proposed by the British and Japanese during the legal rights negotiations issued yesterday had a slight error due to repeated transmission. The original meaning should be "Chinese special courts should try foreign cases with Chinese and foreign judges jointly."

Wang Boqun is Unable to Go to Beijing Due to Illness 169

Yu Feipeng Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Minister of Communications Wang Boqun has been ill in Shanghai for more than half a month. He has repeatedly received telegrams from the central government urging him to go to Beijing, but he has been unable to do so due to his illness. In order to understand the truth, a certain gentleman, accompanied by Shuangqingjun of the Eurasia Aviation Company, went to visit Mr. Wang yesterday afternoon to inquire about the truth. The car arrived at Wang's residence at No. 14 Zhangjia Garden Lane, Jing'an Temple Road, and a red paper strip was posted next to the door, with the words "The illness has not lessened, the doctor advises rest, it is difficult to see guests, please forgive me." The doorman peered out and only then opened the door. Going upstairs to Wang's bedroom, he saw Wang lying on the couch, covered with quilts, with a thick towel wrapped around his forehead. His appearance was thinner and extremely haggard. He was unable to greet the visitor, and then closed his eyes and went to sleep. It was said that his fever was still 101 degrees, so he was extremely tired. The reporter then withdrew. According to reports, Mr. Wang's illness began on the 15th of last month. At first, his legs were in pain. Because it was an old illness, he did not pay much attention to it. The doctor diagnosed it as a flu. The next day, he developed typhoid fever and intestinal heat. At first, he asked German doctor Dr. Lohr, but now he is being treated by Dr. Xu Shifang, and there are two nurses taking turns to take care of him day and night. Last week, he received a telegram from the central government urging him to go to Beijing immediately, and he had prepared a ship on the evening of one day, but unexpectedly his fever rose to 103 degrees on the morning of the second day, so he could not go. Yesterday, he also received a telegram from the Ministry of Communications, reporting that He Yingqin had already taken a warship from Nanchang to the north, and it was expected that he would arrive in Beijing yesterday afternoon.

Also, Minister Wang received a telegram from President Chiang Kai-shek of Nanjing three days ago, which read: "Minister Wang Boqun brother Jian, I heard that you have typhoid fever and have not recovered, I am very concerned. Please rest in peace, and if you recover slightly, please attend the National Assembly, Zheng Zhong Jiang Yin. Deputy Minister of Communications Yu Feipeng also came to Shanghai yesterday to inquire about Mr. Wang's illness."

Local News Two

Apprentice of Qianzhuang Exposed for Illegally Receiving Large Sums of Money 171

As Usual, a Phone Call First

Unexpectedly, This Caused Failure

Dong Niankang, a Ningbo native, 41 years old, has been the manager of Yiyuan Qianzhuang in Jixiang Lane, South City. At noon the day before yesterday, he suddenly received a phone call, claiming to be from Laowenbao Jewelry Store at No. 248 Xinzha Road. The caller stated that the jewelry store needed to pay Runchang Hao 948 yuan and asked him to prepare the funds so that a clerk could be sent to collect them immediately. After listening, Dong was worried that something was wrong, so he made another phone call to the jewelry store to inquire. Dong Xuepeng, the owner of the jewelry store, was shocked when he received the call and immediately rushed to the qianzhuang to meet with Dong Niankang. Dong Xuepeng stated that he had not sent a clerk to collect funds or pay Runchang. While they were talking, a young man of about 20 years old came to the qianzhuang with a blank check from Laowenbao Jewelry Store payable to Runchang Hao, claiming that he wanted to withdraw 948 yuan. At that time, the two Dongs heard about it, stepped out from inside, and observed that they did not recognize the young man. Knowing that he was not a good person, they immediately called the police officer Lu Guangwen from that station to come and detain him, and took him to the First District General Administration for preliminary interrogation. According to his statement, his name was Liu Dianqing, 19 years old, from Yangzhou. He was working as a tea server at the Taian Inn outside the Xinbeimen Gate on Minguo Road. At 9:00 AM today, a young man, claiming to be Zhou Suichu, came to the inn and booked room No. 58. After lunch, he gave me the check and asked me to take it to Yiyuan Qianzhuang to withdraw 948 yuan. He did not know the details. The detectives were immediately dispatched to the inn and arrested Zhou and brought him back for questioning. Zhou stated that he was 18 years old, from Ningbo, and had been an apprentice at Yiyuan Qianzhuang. He was very familiar with the qianzhuang's clients. He was fired in September last year and returned to his hometown. In December, he came to Shanghai again and stayed at the Taixin Inn outside the Xiaodongmen Gate in the French Concession. Because he had no progress and life was difficult, he had to privately carve a seal and fraudulently obtained a passbook from Yiyuan Qianzhuang from Futai Chang. Later, he asked the inn's tea server to take the passbook to Yiyuan Qianzhuang and withdrew 1,500 yuan. However, he was unlucky, and the money was all lost in gambling dens in a few days. His livelihood has become increasingly difficult. He then privately carved the seals of Laowenbao Jewelry Store and Runchang Hao and forged a check, sending the tea server to the qianzhuang to fraudulently obtain 948 yuan for use. He first made a phone call to notify the qianzhuang, impersonating Laowenbao Jewelry Store, as usual, but unexpectedly this caused the failure and he was arrested. He did not deny anything. He was ordered to remain in custody for verification.

Xue Qishi's Finger Amputation Case to be Pronounced 172

Judge Sincerely Urged Reconciliation

The Two Sides Did Not Reach an Agreement and Adjourned

Chen Kengran, the manager of Youlian Film Company, was previously sued in the Special District Court by Xue Qishi, an actor in the company, for intentional injury, with a request for compensation of 29,460 yuan. The next day, Chen also countersued Xue in the Special District Court for crimes such as intimidation and fraud. The details of the initial trial of this case have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday was the second trial of the part of Xue Qishi's lawsuit against Chen Kengran and Zhao Taishan for injury and compensation. Judge Cheng Shangfeng continued the trial. After both sides had finished providing the past situation (the same as before, omitted), Judge Cheng advised the plaintiff, "Filing a lawsuit is a useless thing. It is better to listen to my advice and let Chen pay 300 yuan as consolation, and the two sides will settle the dispute from now on. It is more practical. Moreover, although Zhao Taishan is currently working at Youlian, according to his own confession, his monthly income is only 25 yuan. If he is really found guilty and punished, it will not help you. Xue said that since the injury, he has suffered mentally and physically, and he has become disabled. It is difficult to find a job. Even if he tells his will, he wants to punish Chen first, and then talk about compensation." The judge then asked Chen, "Are you willing to listen to my advice now and give Xue 300 yuan as consolation? You should know that the plaintiff was injured on official duty. Judging from his situation, it is really pitiful. It is not too much to pay some compensation." Chen said that he was willing to follow the instructions and settle peacefully, but the plaintiff had been treated and given money on his behalf since he was injured. Now he has been charged with criminal charges for repeatedly failing to get what he wanted, which is detrimental to his reputation. He was not unhappy in his heart. Even the Youlian Company is not owned by one person and cannot be the master alone. Judge Cheng then advised the plaintiff, "According to your request in the lawsuit, the purpose is nothing more than compensation. Now, for the sake of settling things, it is better to listen to my advice and add another 100 yuan to you, for a total of 400 yuan, and the two sides will settle it." Xue replied, "Since I was injured, I have been unemployed for a long time. Not to mention that I have a lot of debt, even one item of pawn is more than 400 yuan. If I get 400 yuan, I will not be able to pay off my old debts, nor will I be able to clear my debts and return to my hometown. It is difficult to find a job. The small amount of money will be eaten up, which is not helpful." He immediately expressed his unwillingness to accept it and requested that the other party give him a job. Chen Kengran also said, "The plaintiff has no fixed address and has said that he would shoot my family to death and then commit suicide. If this is the case, even if some money is given to comfort him for his injury, if he has unsafe actions against me in the future, he must issue a certificate when this case is settled peacefully, stating that he will not take any harmful actions in the future. As for the position, I have no idea." Because the plaintiff was still unwilling to accept the advice, there was no guarantee of safety. The court immediately asked the lawyers on both sides to begin their arguments. After arguing, the court scheduled the pronouncement of the verdict.

A Depraved Youth Commits Suicide 174

Weak Will and Bad Environment

Gambling and Unemployment Lead to Inability to Extricate Himself

Wang Shuan, a native of Anhui, was only twenty-four years old. Last year, he came to Shanghai from his hometown to seek employment and was hired by the Kunlun Tobacco Company. If he had been able to work diligently, especially as a promising young man, it would not have been difficult for him to rise above others. However, due to his weak will, he was tempted by a bad environment and made many harmful friends. He was devoted to gambling, and his monthly salary was insufficient to cover his reckless bets. As a result, he accumulated heavy debts and was dismissed from his job. He became destitute in Shanghai and had no face to return to his elders in his hometown. Ye Shengwu, a distant relative in Shanghai, repeatedly provided him with financial assistance, but ultimately failed to alleviate his poverty. Wang's situation became increasingly dire, exacerbated by creditor harassment and an empty wallet. Feeling that there was no joy in life, he went alone to a large hotel on Jiujiang Road on the afternoon of the second of this month, falsely claiming to be lodging there. After being led by a waiter to Room 31, he closed the door and drafted two suicide notes, stating that since losing his job, his finances had become increasingly strained, and he had accumulated hundreds of dollars in gambling debts, all borrowed, with no way to repay them, hence his suicide. He also wrote ten letters to relatives and friends who had lent him money, expressing his inability to repay the loans in this life and hoping to do so in the next, apologizing profusely and hoping for understanding. After completing these preparations, he ingested poison and waited in bed to die. The next day, near noon, when a waiter wanted to enter the room to clean, he knocked on the door but received no response. He broke down the door and opened the curtains to check, only to find that Wang's face had turned gray, and he was no longer breathing, having died at an unknown time. The hotel staff immediately reported to the Zhabei Police Station, which dispatched detective Zhang Yi to investigate. After an investigation, the body was taken to the forensic examination office on Faelun Road, and the suicide notes were taken back to the police station. His relative, Ye Shengwu, was also notified. Yesterday morning, Ye went to the morgue, awaiting Qian, a prosecutor from the Special District Court, to arrive for a clear examination before requesting to claim the body for burial. This was approved. It is said that one wrong step leads to a thousand regrets, and it is too late to turn back. This can be used as a lament for Wang Shuan. Many young people are like Wang, and they should wake up to this reality.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau Re-emphasizes the Prohibition of Usury and Exploitation 175

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating that usury and exploitation harm people's livelihoods and must be strictly prohibited. The Central Political Conference resolved in its 111th meeting in the 16th year of the Republic that the maximum interest rate should not exceed 20% per annum, and the Municipal Government's Notice No. 5 and the Bureau's orders to its subordinates have been issued to comply with this. Fearing that the matter may be taken lightly over time, and unscrupulous individuals may still be engaging in double-dealing and exploiting the poor, the prohibition must be reiterated and strictly enforced. In addition to ordering subordinates to pay attention to and prohibit this at any time, this notice is issued for compliance. From now on, the prescribed interest rate must be strictly implemented, and usury and exploitation are prohibited. Anyone who dares to violate this will be punished according to the law once discovered and will not be tolerated. This notice is issued on May 4th.

Bicycle Also Badly Damaged

Petition from Rickshaw Pullers in West Shanghai 178

Requesting the Public Works Bureau to Organize Matters Gradually

Peng Yuzhi, Sun Zhaokang, Yu Hainan, Li Zhiliang, Tang Changyu, and more than twenty other representatives of rickshaw pullers in West Shanghai submitted a petition to the Municipal Government yesterday, stating that they had received Public Works Bureau's approval number 449, acknowledging their submission. The case had been previously submitted to the Bureau by Tai Jiangzhou and others, and on April 15th, an order was issued to register in accordance with the regulations announced by the Finance Bureau and the Bureau. Their request to issue licenses based on the original number and to use old vehicles was deemed unnecessary. Upon receiving this, the petitioners were deeply distressed, as their families depended on the rickshaws for their livelihood, lacking savings and skills. The Municipal Government's proposal to increase the number of rickshaws was intended for those who wanted to be self-employed and own their vehicles. Therefore, they expressed their difficulties and hardships, requesting the Public Works Bureau to issue licenses based on the original number of rickshaws, considering the livelihood of the poor while organizing traffic. They had no intention of being deceptive or opportunistic. The facts were clear and easily verifiable. However, they were repeatedly rejected without any flexibility. Upon investigation, the rickshaws operating in the Chinese area were mostly淘汰ed from the public concession and some were broken old chartered rickshaws mixed among them when the initial organization華界 was still a pioneering effort It was feared that they would wait and see, and those who came would be granted licenses. After three years of inspection, the uneven vehicles were gradually淘汰ed. Therefore, the 7,400 rickshaws in South Shanghai and Zhabei were more 整齊 and presentable than those in West Shanghai, and only a small number were completely renovated. As the West Shanghai market was still under construction, the rickshaw pullers were not comparable to those who operated for companies. Since the government was able to accommodate them in the past, it should show even more compassion and generosity to these four hundred or so scattered rickshaw pullers, showing its genuine intention to help the poor. The government has been building affordable housing for the people, repeatedly showing its concern for the poor. The rickshaw pullers, who are located in the corner of the city, are the poorest among the people. How dare they dream of building mansions. This request for increased licensing and organization is entirely in accordance with the government's intentions. They will still implement the Public Works Bureau's plan to increase the number of rickshaws in order, with only slight variations in timing based on local conditions. There is no harm to the public, nor to private interests. They earnestly request the Municipal Government to instruct the Public Works Bureau to organize matters gradually within its ability, to save lives and maintain public welfare. They are anxiously awaiting orders.

Zhang Shisheng, a Renowned Figure in Traditional Chinese Medicine, Has Passed Away 179

Shanghai Medical and Pharmaceutical Communities Prepare for Memorial Service

Mr. Zhang Shisheng of Haimen dedicated himself to the study of Chinese medicine for nearly thirty years. His experience and knowledge were highly respected in the medical field. He served as the President of the Haimen County Medical and Pharmaceutical Research Association in Jiangsu, the Principal of the Zhongxing Medical and Pharmaceutical Vocational School, the Chairman of the Haimen County Branch of the National Medical and Pharmaceutical Association of Jiangsu Province, a professor of pharmaceutical quality at the Shanghai Chinese Medicine Vocational School, the Chinese Medical College, and the National Medical College, and an executive member and standing committee member of the National Medical and Pharmaceutical Organizations Federation. He donated a large sum of money to establish the National Medical and Pharmaceutical Association's Drug Exhibition Center and invested solely in developing a medicinal herb garden in Nanxiang to cultivate domestic medicinal plants for experimentation and improvement. In summary, he made significant contributions to Chinese medicine and pharmaceuticals and was deeply admired by the medical and pharmaceutical communities at home and abroad. Last winter, Mr. Zhang represented the National Medical and Pharmaceutical Association to urge the establishment of the Central National Pharmaceutical Museum. During the severe winter, Mr. Zhang braved the snow, resulting in a cold. He became ill upon his return, and after more than two months of illness, despite the careful diagnosis and treatment of famous Chinese and Western doctors, he passed away in his hometown on the first day of the third month of the lunar calendar at the age of fifty-five. The news of his passing has been met with widespread mourning. It is now learned that Ding Zhongying, Xie Liheng, Xia Yingtang, Zhang Meian, Cai Jiping, Jiang Wenfang, Bao Shisheng, Xu Xiangren, Yu Botao, Shen Zhuoru, Fu Yongyan, Huang Baozhong, Qin Bowei, and Yan Cangshan, all well-known figures in the Shanghai Chinese medicine and pharmaceutical communities, as well as the National Medical and Pharmaceutical Association, the Shanghai Municipal Chinese Medicine Association, the National Pharmaceutical Association, the Chinese Medicine Vocational School, the National Medical College, and the Chinese Medical College, believe that Mr. Zhang devoted his life to medicine and pharmaceuticals and made irreplaceable contributions. They plan to jointly organize a memorial service and have decided to establish a memorial service preparatory committee at the Shanghai Municipal Chinese Medicine Association, Room 24, 2nd Floor, Yizhong Company Building, Zhejiang Road, Shanghai. Zhang Meian, Jiang Wenfang, and Shen Tingdong will be responsible for the preparations. Once the preparations are complete, a public memorial service will be held on a selected day.

Sentencing for Child Abduction 181

Two Years and Six Months Imprisonment Each

When Wang A Ming's son Mao Jian was still a baby, he was sent to the home of Luo Guangxiu's wife Wang, fellow villagers living at 299 Tangjiawan in the French Concession, for breastfeeding and care. After two years, A Ming took him back. The child is now four years old. On the morning of the 2nd of this month, Luo went to Wang's home in Hele Lane, North Henan Road, and enticed Mao Jian with candy, taking him out with him. Luo's wife, Wang, was waiting at the alley entrance and immediately picked up the child, hired a rickshaw, and fled. Li Ada, Wang's neighbor, witnessed the incident and reported it to A Ming, who reported it to the Hongkou Police Station. Detectives were dispatched to Luo's home and arrested Luo and his wife. However, Mao Jian was nowhere to be found. Under strict questioning, Luo and his wife confessed that they had hidden him at the home of their subtenant, Yang Zhong. The detectives then arrested Yang. The child was first returned to A Ming. Yesterday morning, Luo and the other three men and women were brought to the Special District Court for trial. Luo and his wife admitted to taking the child, but claimed that Yang Zhong had recently lost her son and was crying all day, so they took Mao Jian to her home, intending to sell him as an adopted son, but the deal had not been completed. Yang Zhong confessed that she had intended to buy him as an adopted son, but she still needed to investigate his background. The police lawyer argued that the three defendants were undoubtedly guilty of child abduction and requested that they be severely punished. After questioning, Judge Feng sentenced each of them to two years and six months of imprisonment. The three convicts all bowed their heads in submission and were sent to prison.

Verdict Announced in the Case of the Maid Run Over by a Car 182

Compensation of 1,200 Yuan to the Deceased's Family

Gu, the mother of Teng Shisheng, a native of Dang Ri in Suzhou, worked as a servant at the Southeast Building Emblem Hall on Dongxinqiao Street in the French Concession. On the morning of the 17th of last month, at 9:00 AM, she went out to buy vegetables. At the intersection of Dongxinqiao Vegetable Market Street, a French-owned tram driven by Luo Bingzhang collided with a cart pulled by Xu Baoxing of the Dahe Coal Company, causing Gu to be struck and killed. Subsequently, her son, represented by lawyer Yan Feixi Zhen, filed a complaint with the French Court, requesting compensation of 5,000 yuan. After questioning by the Chinese and Western officials, a verdict was awaited. Yesterday, the Chinese and Western officials issued an order after the Mingtang hearing, summoning both parties. The verdict stated that after investigation by the Court, the case was found to be true. The defendant, Luo Bingzhang, was fined 20 yuan, and Xu Baoxing of the Dahe Coal Company was fined 10 yuan. They were also jointly ordered to compensate the plaintiff's family with a funeral compensation of 1,200 yuan. Luo Bingzhang was responsible for one-third, and the Dahe Coal Company was responsible for two-thirds.

The Minsheng Warship Launches Today 190

Ceremony at 3:00 PM

The Ministry of the Navy has been successively building new warships since 1928, including the Xianning, Yongsui, Minquan, and Yixian. The hull of the fifth ship, the Minsheng, has now been completed. The launching ceremony is scheduled for 3:00 PM today at the Jiangnan Shipyard in Gaochangmiao. The details are as follows:

Ceremony Order 191

(1) All attendees take their seats; (2) Music is played; (3) The Party song is sung; (4) All attendees bow three times to the Party flag, the national flag, and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen; (5) The chairman respectfully reads Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will; (6) The launching ceremony is held; (7) Music is played; (8) The chairman delivers an opening address; (9) A representative of the Central Party Headquarters delivers an address; (10) A representative of the National Government delivers an address; (11) A representative of the Executive Yuan delivers an address; (12) A representative of the Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force delivers an address; (13) A representative of the Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force delivers an address; (14) Guests deliver speeches; (15) The chairman replies; (16) Slogans are shouted: "Long live the Kuomintang of China," "Long live the Republic of China," "Long live the National Government," "Long live the revolutionary navy," "Long live the Minsheng warship"; (17) The ceremony concludes; (18) Music is played; (19) Photographs are taken; (20) Refreshments are served.

Minsheng Details 192

The Minsheng is a gunboat that will be assigned to the Second Fleet. It is 205 feet long, 26 feet wide, and has a draft of 6 feet. It has two sets of triple expansion steam engines and two water-tube boilers, with a horsepower of 2,400 and a speed of 18 nautical miles per hour. It has a displacement of 505 tons. It is equipped with two 12-pounder guns, one 3-inch anti-aircraft gun, two 5.7-pounder quick-firing guns, one 2-pounder anti-aircraft gun, and six 30-caliber 79 water-cooled machine guns. The keel was laid on November 10th of last year, and it is scheduled to be completed in August of this year. It is valued at 1.5 million yuan.

Glimpse of the Arrangement 193

Yesterday afternoon, the members of the Supervision Office and the Navy Special Party Department arranged everything at the ceremonial ground. The ground is located south of the shipyard, and the ceremonial platform is in the shape of an A. The center is the rostrum, with the guest platform on both sides. Slogans and naval flags of various countries are displayed. The center in front of the rostrum is the Minsheng. The bow of the ship faces the platform, and the stern faces the Huangpu River. The bottom is painted red ocher, the middle is white, and the top is apricot red. Pine, cypress, paper flowers, and flags of various countries are hung on it. The Party flag and national flag are hung on the left and right of the bow.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Exemption from Business Tax on Outbound Boxed Tea 200

To Facilitate Overseas Sales of Chinese Tea

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing yesterday, stating that the Shanghai Foreign Tea Industry Association had stated that its business was declining due to the export of tea from India, Ceylon, Java, and Japan. The export of tea in those countries, were lightly taxed if not exempted, and various subsidies were provided to seize the sales of Chinese tea. In October of the 8th year of the Republic, domestic Li Jin tax was reduced by 50% or exempted. Request was made in previous years to exempt them, the government exempted Li Jin tax immediately and the request was not repeated. Now that the Li Jin tax has been completely exempted, outbound boxed tea is subject to the same business tax as general merchandise. However, Anhui Province suddenly announced that outbound boxed tea would be subject to a business tax of 20 per mille, the same as general merchandise. The Association telegraphed the Ministry of Finance requesting the Anhui Finance Department to exempt the tax, but has not received a reply. The request is made to the Ministry of Finance, requesting the government to permanently exempt outbound boxed tea from customs duties, business taxes, and miscellaneous taxes under other names, to maintain the export of domestic products. Given this, the export of Chinese tea has been exempted from customs duties with approval. As the tea industry has been severely impacted by Indian and Ceylon teas, taxes and duties should be further reduced to protect the industry. Although business tax is a commercial tax, the lace embroidery industry has been exempted from business tax due to its focus on foreign trade. The Association had telegraphed in request and was issued with 钧批赋字 No. 12145 stating that the nature of the lace embroidery business focuses on foreign trade and differs from ordinary lace industry, the request for exemption of business tax is justified. The intention to promote the export of domestic goods is evident. The promotion of Chinese tea exports is of greater importance than lace embroidery, and business tax should be exempted to facilitate development. The request is made to the Ministry for approval. It is a matter of public convenience. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce kowtows.

Municipal Finance Bureau Takes Over the Municipal Slaughter Tax 201

The Municipal Finance Bureau previously submitted a request to the Municipal Government, which was forwarded to the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office regarding the municipal slaughter tax, which was being collected by them. The request instructed a prompt handover and takeover. It is now heard that the negotiations have been completed. Recently, the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office sent a letter to the Municipal Government, scheduling the collection by our municipality to begin on the first of this month. Upon receiving the order, the Municipal Finance Bureau immediately began preparing for all takeover matters and drafted regulations for the collection of the slaughter tax. After submitting them to the Municipal Government for approval, they will be jointly announced with the Health Bureau. All pig and sheep slaughterhouses within the municipal area must comply with these collection regulations, purchase tax tickets in advance, and be prepared for inspection. It is also heard that the veterinarians dispatched by the Health Bureau and the accountants dispatched by the Finance Bureau have been appointed. The regulations are as follows: Attached are the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau's Slaughter Tax Collection Regulations: Article 1: The slaughter tax listed in these regulations is temporarily established for pigs and sheep. All pig and sheep slaughterhouses in the municipal area must comply. Article 2: The slaughter tax is collected by the various collection offices under this Bureau. Article 3: The slaughter tax rates are as follows: (A) Tax of 39 cents (大洋) per pig slaughtered. (B) Tax of 20 cents (大洋) per sheep slaughtered. Article 4: Each slaughterhouse should purchase slaughter tax tickets in advance, categorized, from the collection offices established by this Bureau in the nearby area. The ticket format will be determined separately. Article 5: The types of slaughter tax tickets are as follows: (A) Pig slaughter tax ticket: white, 39 cents (大洋) per ticket, 50 tickets per book, totaling 19.50 (大洋). (B) Sheep slaughter tax ticket: blue, 20 cents (大洋) per ticket, 50 tickets per book, totaling 10 (大洋). Article 6: Daily, this Bureau will dispatch personnel during pig and sheep slaughter inspection hours to go to each slaughterhouse with the Health Bureau inspectors to check the number of slaughtered animals. Article 7: Each slaughterhouse should present the tax tickets for verification according to the number of pigs and sheep slaughtered daily. The accountants from this Bureau will clip the corners and cancel them. Article 8: If no tax ticket is found for the pigs and sheep slaughtered by each slaughterhouse, they should be ordered to purchase and present the tax tickets for inspection before being allowed to transport them out of the factory. Those who conceal the number of slaughtered animals will be fined three times the amount of tax payable in addition to making up the tax. Article 9: Any slaughterhouse that resists inspection will be sent to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. Article 10: If any accounting personnel of this Bureau extort or engage in favoritism and malpractice, they will be investigated and dealt with according to law upon discovery or accusation. Article 11: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be submitted for amendment at any time. Article 12: These regulations will be implemented from the date of approval by the Municipal Government.

Representatives of the Cattle, Sheep, and Pig Industries Petition the Municipal Government and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce 202

Abolish Inspection Fees

The cattle, sheep, and pig industries in our municipality are burdened by the Municipal Finance Bureau's collection of slaughter tax, inspection fees, and the upcoming municipal business tax. The merchants and residents of these industries feel that they cannot bear such overlapping charges. Yesterday (the 4th), they selected five general representatives: Chen Baosheng, Shen Liansheng, Lu Yichen, Gu Changsheng, and He Rusheng. (It was said that they originally intended to send the entire group, but due to the Memorial Day, they feared the government might misunderstand, so they changed to sending representatives.) They submitted petitions to the Municipal Government and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. The Municipal Government only received the petition, as the Mayor was in Beijing and Secretary-General Yu was on official business, and did not grant an audience. They then went to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, where Mr. Zheng received them. The representatives explained that the cattle, sheep, and pig industries consist of small merchants and residents, and now the Finance Bureau only knows how to collect money without considering the suffering of the merchants and residents. (The cost of a goat is about 20 cents (小洋), but it has to be taxed 27 cents (大洋), which is actually a tax of 150%. The tax on cattle and pigs is also above 10%, with a tax of about 30% or more on small cattle.) Since the collection of cattle and sheep inspection fees began, the industry has suffered greatly. For example, the cattle and sheep industry association is using the excuse that the Municipal Finance Bureau is recovering the extra inspection fees for cattle and sheep from 1919 and is ordering the industry to retroactively pay the fees, which is unbearable. Therefore, the public is indignant and compelled to state the facts and reasons, appealing to the government to abolish the inspection fees for livestock, which are similar to a transit tax and should be abolished. The National Government is now streamlining and abolishing excessive levies and miscellaneous taxes to alleviate the people's difficulties. We in the pig, cattle, and sheep industries are all citizens under the blue and white flag and should enjoy the right to "one item, one tax." Since the business tax is about to be implemented, our industry should not be an exception. Once the business tax is levied, the inspection and slaughter items should be abolished immediately in accordance with the National Government's order. Moreover, the cattle, sheep, and pigs slaughtered before slaughter are transported to the concession for slaughter. When slaughtering in the concession, it is necessary to pay the slaughterhouse fee. It is not possible to establish inspection items and collect huge handling fees just because they pass through the Chinese territory. Inspection should be implemented because it is related to meat hygiene and cannot be abolished. If the Municipal Health Bureau needs funds for hiring veterinarians for inspection and other inspection parts and cannot make up for the expenses, then our industry is willing to be responsible for the sanitation expenses of the livestock inspection part. Please forward the request to the government to open a low budget for the sanitation expenses of the livestock inspection in 1920 and assign it to the cattle, sheep, and pig industries to share. In this way, the government will not have to abandon eating due to choking, and the merchants and residents can avoid worrying all day long. Please, your association, accurately forward the request, etc. Mr. Zheng of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce replied that the request from your industry to forward various situations is justified and the Chamber will do so. The representatives then left.

Airline Company Cables the United States to Purchase Aircraft 203

The China National Aviation Corporation (中國航空公司) faces the obstruction of high mountains in Sichuan, causing inconvenient transportation. Mail between Shanghai and Chengdu takes more than ten days to arrive. The company recently expanded its air routes to complete its original plan, extending the Shanghai-Yichang line to Wanxian and Chongqing. There are dangerous gorges between Wanxian, requiring light and convenient airplanes to fly over the gorges more nimbly. The company telegraphed the Curtiss airplane factory in the United States to order four light Loening airplanes, which are expected to arrive in Shanghai in about a month. The airport sites in Wanxian and Chongqing have been surveyed and found suitable. The wireless radio to be installed in the station building will be installed by engineers dispatched by the company after the American aircraft arrive in Shanghai.

The National Goods Maintenance Association Promotes the Korean National Products Exhibition Hall 204

The Chinese National Goods Maintenance Association (中華國貨維持會) has recently been actively working to promote the Korean National Products Exhibition Hall, sparing no effort. Because Zhang Weicheng, the Consul-General stationed in Korea, is about to return to his post, the Association plans to collect samples of domestic national product factories and transfer them to Consul Zhang to Korea, so that they can be displayed as soon as possible. Yesterday, a notice was issued to various national silk and satin industries and cotton weaving factories to urge them to submit the samples. The original text is as follows: (Omitted above) It is found that the amount of goods shipped from our country to Korea reached several tens of millions of dollars in the past. However, since Japan implemented harsh levies on Chinese goods, with a tax of 100% of the value, only a few items could be shipped, and most of the silk and satin goods have not been able to be shipped in inches or threads for many years. Hundreds of thousands of people in our country's industrial and commercial circles have been destroyed by it. Although the government has worked hard to negotiate and amended it to 70% of the value, it is still too far from the 8% of the value levied on Japanese goods. Fortunately, the agreement is for a period of three years, excluding the past year, there are only two years left. The Association plans to take advantage of this period to request the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to convene relevant industrial and commercial groups to study in detail the points that should be amended in this Sino-Japanese commercial agreement, so as to submit them to Japan for negotiation and proper handling. On the other hand, with the consent of Mr. Zhang Weicheng, the Consul-General stationed in Korea, samples of our country's fine national goods will be collected and sent to the Consulate-General stationed in Korea. A Chinese National Goods Exhibition Hall will be established on a selected site, so that overseas Chinese and local people from all walks of life can be invited to visit the hall from time to time, so that they can understand and recognize it, and develop their belief and purchase intention. This is the first step in preparing for the restoration of the trade in Korea. Moreover, Consul Zhang is returning to China on official business and will stay in Shanghai for several days. Therefore, this special letter is delivered, and we ask your office to quickly compile the fine old and new goods samples, compile the numbers, and open the name of the factory, address, trademark, value, and other words on another paper. Deliver the properly packaged goods to the Association's office for inspection before the 25th of this month, so that they can be transferred to Consul Zhang to Korea for display, restore the inherent honor, and recreate the glory of the country. (Omitted below), etc.

The Business Tax Preparatory Office Scheduled to Continue the Meeting 205

Three Principles Previously Agreed

The municipal business tax, which is being handled by the business tax preparatory office, drafted a draft of the collection regulations and implementation rules, as well as the tax standard and tax rate table. (On the 1st of this month, representatives of the Chamber of Commerce, Wang Yansong, etc., were convened to participate in the discussion. It is heard that only three major principles were agreed on that day: (1) The Chinese and foreign concessions should be levied uniformly, (2) Chinese and foreign stores should be treated equally, and (3) The tax rate principle should be separately set at three levels: 1/1000, 2/1000, and 3/1000. It is necessary to ask the Municipal Government for instructions before a decision can be made. However, for the convenience of current research, the representatives of the Chamber of Commerce can temporarily use it as a standard when reviewing the draft tax rate. The next session is scheduled for the 21st of this month and will still be held at the preparatory office.

"A Wife Joins the Army" to be Released Tomorrow 206

The military love film "A Wife Joins the Army," produced by Zhang Shichuan of the Star Film Company and co-directed by Tang Jie and Wang Jiting, is scheduled to be released day and night on the 3rd of this month at the Central Grand Theater on Six Malu. The film stars Gong Jianong and Liang Saizhen, and is performed by all male and female stars. It was previewed once and the results were excellent. It is expected that the box office will be excellent. It is also heard that the film "Sea of Hatred," co-directed by Gao Lihen and Tan Zhiyuan of the company, has been completed. The results of the film screening are also very satisfactory. The release date is not far away.

Sincere Company Promotes Eau de Cologne 207

Eau de cologne, made by Sincere Company, is an essential product for summer families. The fragrance is fragrant and the function is to ward off dirt, refresh the brain, refresh and relieve boredom, and treat mosquito bites. The excellence of the product is enough to resist imports and is deeply appreciated by the Chinese. It is heard that the company, in order to promote national goods, is preparing a large sacrifice of 100,000 yuan. Therefore, when raw materials are rising day by day, only old goods are sold to reward the enthusiasm of patriotic gentlemen. Customer assistance doors and markets have been buying in large quantities for days, which shows the enthusiasm of the social people to promote national goods.

Yiuseng Travel Troupe Photography Exhibition Opens 208

The Yiuseng Travel Troupe's travel photography exhibition opened yesterday. In addition to scenic spots in China, there are also landscapes and monuments in Siam, Japan, Switzerland, India, and other places, which are full of products and extremely collected. In addition to the team members, there were about 500 guests. It is expected that the number of visitors will be more enthusiastic in the next two days.

Xuangong Western Restaurant Opens Tomorrow 209

Xuangong Western Restaurant at the intersection of Zhejiang Road and Tianjin Road is scheduled to open tomorrow (6th). It is heard that in addition to carefully making Western food, the restaurant also hires a professional technician to make Chinese and Western famous dishes and various nutritious foods. Everything is done to be clean and beneficial to health. In order to facilitate customers, various teas and snacks are sold in the morning and midnight, and the prices are very low.

The Effectiveness of the National Natural Fertilizer Powder 210

Seagull Trademark National Natural Fertilizer Powder is produced by the China Agricultural and Mining Company. Its material is rich in natural fertilizer, and its effectiveness is completely different from those made by chemical methods. After repeated experiments, it has achieved great success. The company has now added an office at No. 235 Sichuan Road.

The Initiation of the Wuyuan Alumni Association 211

The number of young people from Wuyuan studying in Shanghai's major universities is increasing. Unfortunately, there is no perfect organization to connect them, resulting in a scattered situation in the same place. Recently, Shi Wenmo and Hu Zhongjie, who live in Shanghai, felt the necessity of establishing a group, and initiated the Wuyuan Shanghai Alumni Friendship Association to connect feelings and cooperate with each other. On May 10th, a dinner party will be held in the Western Restaurant of the YMCA on North Sichuan Road to discuss the progress steps and welcome students from Wuyuan in various schools to participate.

"Western Hermaphrodite" Premieres in Paris 212

The Paris Grand Theater on Avenue Joffre premiered the extraordinary and giant film "Western Hermaphrodite" starring German superstar Walter Rilla yesterday morning. The film's deification of performance and the compactness of the plot are like huge waves of the river and sea, rolling in and making people feel agitated. The strangeness of the material is even more unprecedented on the screen, which is quite similar to the strange case recently reported in Chinese and Western newspapers that a certain German man specializes in raping and killing women. It is heard that the film is scheduled to be released in the theater this Thursday.

Church of Our Savior Welcomes Representatives of the General Assembly 213

The Church of Our Savior of the Chinese Holy Catholic Church held a welcome service for the representatives of the 7th General Assembly of the Chinese Holy Catholic Church in the church at 10 am yesterday. The weather was clear and the breeze was warm. The church was full of flowers and green cypresses. The educational flags were hung on the walls, dazzling. No less than a thousand Chinese and Western men and women, as well as national representatives, attended the church for worship. Those who arrived later had no place to stand, so it was very crowded. All the etiquette was solemn and grand. First, Dr. Zhu Baoyuan, the regional shepherd, led the Chinese bishops and representatives from various provinces to the Holy of Holies in white robes for a grand worship service and administered the Eucharist until 12 o'clock. After the ceremony, a banquet of ten tables was held in the dining hall of the church until 2:30 pm.

The General Assembly of the Chinese Holy Catholic Church Closes 214

The 7th General Assembly of the Chinese Holy Catholic Church closed. The thanksgiving worship service was held at Trinity Church on Third Malu yesterday. There was a large crowd of church members. Dr. Zhu Baoyuan of the Church of Our Savior in Hongkou presided over the ceremony. The order is as follows: (1) The whole body sings hymn 336, (2) Dr. Zhu Baoyuan read the entire evening prayer, and Pastor Shen Si'en read Psalm 24, (3) Pastor Dai Diao Hou read Ephesians 4:1-16 from the New Testament and sang a hymn, (4) Pastor Yao Xianyang recited the Apostle's Creed and sang a hymn, (5) Deputy Bishop Shen Zaisheng of the Zhejiang Chinese preached and collected donations, (6) The pastor of Trinity Church blessed and sang a hymn before adjourning. It was already half past four.

Sun Shihao's Solo Exhibition 215

The famous painter Sun Junshihao was good at painting in his childhood. Later, he traveled to France, Belgium, Italy, and other countries, and his studies became more refined. When he held solo exhibitions in Berlin, Beijing, Paris, and other places, he was deeply praised by the people of the country. Recently, Mr. Sun returned to China from Europe. This week, he borrowed the scientific society on Avenue Albert in the French Concession to hold a solo exhibition. There are as many as 200 pieces of work, both Chinese and Western paintings, which are extremely exquisite and spectacular. There is a painting of Sun Yat-sen, an old work, with a title by Mr. Cai Yuanpei, which says, "The hunger and drowning of all parties is to be stopped by oneself, and one goes to save them barefooted and bareheaded. Picking up the Three People's Principles, the world will see Datong." And the title by the deceased Mr. Tan Zu'an says, "Water is deep and the fire is hot, alas, the people are so miserable. Who will save them? It is the virtuous man. Blue sky and white sun, see and hear together." In recent days, many people have gone to the meeting to visit, and they all praised Mr. Sun's works in unison.

News from Trade Associations

Shaoxing Wine Industry 216

The Shaoxing Wine Industry Association held its seventh executive committee meeting yesterday afternoon. Chairman Ding Jinsheng performed the ceremony as usual and reported on the previous proposals: (1) It was proposed that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce notify the annual membership fees for the 20th year, which will be prepared by the executive committee members, (2) The industry rules of the industry were drafted by lawyer Wu, selected 14 articles, passed, and copied to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for review, (3) New membership certificates, in addition to reporting to the superior, will be given in accordance with the association's discipline, (4) The license tax issue will be contacted with other associations to act in unison, (5) The association's premises are entirely for office use, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce is requested to transfer it to the Finance Bureau to exempt the house donation case, (6) Tang Peisun was designated as the representative to attend in the 20th year, (7) Each executive committee member is fully responsible for soliciting donations for disaster relief in Shaanxi, (8) The association received the Social Affairs Bureau's certificate No. 62, and a seal was reported to the party and government for record, (9) Zhang Wanrun broke the price list several times, refused to be reconciled, and did not join the association, which is harmful to the industry's business. In addition to reporting to the superiors for investigation, corresponding countermeasures will be taken, (10) The transportation company added freight charges. Each executive committee member proposed not to do so and notified all members of the city to pay according to the original price, otherwise the association will submit it to the superior for handling. The above ten items were unanimously resolved and passed. There are still various items, and the time relationship is not resolved. They will be retained for later mention. The meeting adjourned at 7 o'clock.

Restaurant Industry 217

The Restaurant Industry Association convened its 13th Standing Committee meeting at 2 pm yesterday. Chairman Cheng Kefan reported on the letters from various places. Discussion matters: (1) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce's letter is for the Municipal Party Headquarters' Civil Training Association to fill out the form, and it was resolved to do so, (2) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce's letter is for the Municipal Chamber of Commerce membership fee payable in the 20th year, and the report on the representative case was resolved to do so and notified all members to check, (3) The case of the French patrol's unprovoked shooting of Xin Haishan, please assist, and it was resolved unanimously to advocate, (4) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce came to allow the transfer of the case of reducing business tax, (5) Omitted, (6) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce forwarded the report form of the general survey issued by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and it was decided to fill in the total amount of operating capital of each business before August and resolved to do so. The rest are omitted. The meeting adjourned.

Electrical Appliance Industry 218

The Electrical Appliance Industry Association held its fifth preparatory meeting yesterday. Wang Rongchang, Yuan Yongding, Ding Dixin, Zhao Luqing, Zhu Mingdao, Yu Huanzhang, etc. attended. Chairman Wang Rongchang passed the motions, (1) The inaugural meeting will be held on May 11th, (2) The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce will be the venue for the general meeting, (3) Wang Rongchang, Yuan Yongding, Ding Dixin, Zhao Luqing, Li Henglin, etc. were appointed as the presidium of the general meeting, (4) The expenses of the general meeting will be raised by the finance committee members, (5) The Municipal Party Headquarters, Civil Training Association, Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, and Municipal Chamber of Commerce were requested to send personnel to guide, (6) A letter was sent to various colleagues to fly a flag on the day of the general meeting to celebrate, (7) A notice will be published in the newspaper three days before the general meeting. The meeting adjourned.

Weather Report 219

The Xujiahui Observatory predicted the weather at 4:30 pm yesterday. The weather in the Yangtze River basin and the coast here is uncertain. There are thunderstorms and strong vortices due to the large low pressure in central China moving to the northeast and east. The wind on the Shandong coast and in the Taiwan Strait has increased and is undirected. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 pm yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 75.9 and the lowest was 59.0. On the same day last year, the highest was 78.8 and the lowest was 59.5.

Leshan Doctor in the alley opposite Huaxingji at the southern end of Wangping Street, Sima Road, declares that the doctor specializes in treating coughs and is very effective. All those who suffer from multiple coughs and lung injuries, chronic coughs and tuberculosis, hemoptysis and shortness of breath, etc., once diagnosed and treated, often return to life.

Publishing News 222

Malaya Bookstore declares that the store has been established for several months and has published many new books that sell well in various ports in Southeast Asia. Recently, it has also published Ba Jin's translation of Gorky's "Prairie Story," "Night in the Park" by Zeng Jinke, and "Shadow" translated by Ni Li. Zhang Ruogu's "From Xiao E to Lu Xun," Mao Yibo's "Cherry Blossom Season," Zeng Ke's "The Trilogy of Love," etc. will be published soon. The store has established a distribution office in Ipoh, Malaya, and has now sent personnel to Singapore to establish a branch. Zhu Meizi, the editor-in-chief of the store, has gone to Southeast Asia to contact various overseas Chinese schools and plans to compile textbooks suitable for use in primary and secondary schools for overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia. The editorial department is now headed by Zeng Jinke. The "Malaya Semimonthly," which is also published by Zeng Jun, is also edited by Zeng Jun.

(1) Please indicate the Shanghai Market Department when sending manuscripts from various merchants, doctors, film companies, theaters, and painters.

(2) Please stamp the manuscripts sent by various merchants, film companies, theaters, painters, and doctors as a proof, otherwise they will not be published.

(3) As usual, a small fee is paid for long film manuscripts, calculated at two yuan per thousand words.
